Aapka goal clear hai — Wazuh manager 192.168.1.77 pe setup hai, aur aapko custom
dashboard banana hai jo Wazuh API se data fetch kare. Aap VS Code use kar rahe hain
Windows machine (192.168.1.120) se, jo same internal network mein hai.
Chaliye, main step-by-step flow explain karta hoon — no extra fluff, sirf practical flow.
🔁  Overall Flow (Simplified)
Aapka custom dashboard (frontend/backend) →  Wazuh Manager API (port 55000) se
baat karega.
🧱  Step-by-Step Implementation Flow
✅  Step 1: Wazuh API Access Ready Karna (192.168.1.77)
Wazuh manager ke paas already REST API hoti hai. Aapko bas credentials chahiye.
API base URL hogi: https://192.168.1.77:55000
⚠  Default self-signed certificate hota hai, to aapko ya to rejectUnauthorized: false
karna padega (dev only) ya certificate trust karna hoga.
✅  Step 2: Authentication Flow samjhein
text
[Custom Dashboard UI]
        |
        | HTTP/HTTPS API calls
        ↓
[Wazuh Server Manager - 192.168.1.77:55000]
        |
        | Internally queries
        ↓
[Wazuh Manager + Agents DB]
bash
# Wazuh server (192.168.1.77) pe SSH karke check karein:
cd /var/ossec/api/configuration/auth
cat user  # default: wazuh
cat pass  # default: wazuh (change if needed)

✅  Step 4: Project Structure (Option B — Recommended Safe Flow)
Kyun backend proxy?
Browser se direct API call CORS error degi
Credentials secure rahenge (backend se call)
Aap Wazuh certificate issues easily handle kar sakte hain
✅  Step 5: Backend Proxy Code (Node.js on your Windows machine)
backend/server.js:
text
POST /security/user/authenticate
{
  "username": "wazuh",
  "password": "wazuh"
}
→ Returns JWT token
→ Use token: Authorization: Bearer <token>
Option Description Kaise karein
A. Simple Frontend-only
(HTML/JS)
Ek basic HTML page jo
directly API fetch kare
VS Code se index.html
banao, browser se kholo
B. Full Stack
(React/Node)
Proper dashboard app
(recommended)
VS Code mein project setup
karo, backend proxy banao
text
wazuh-dashboard/
├── backend/
│   ├── server.js        (Node/Express - API proxy)
│   └── .env             (Wazuh credentials)
└── frontend/
    └── src/             (React/Vue or plain HTML)
javascript
const express = require('express');
const axios = require('axios');
const https = require('https');
const cors = require('cors');
require('dotenv').config();
const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
const WAZUH_API = 'https://192.168.1.77:55000';
const agent = new https.Agent({ rejectUnauthorized: false });

✅  Step 6: Frontend Example Call
Aapka frontend (React ya plain HTML from VS Code) aise call karega:
✅  Step 7: Useful Wazuh API Endpoints (Dashboard widgets ke liye)
✅  Step 8: Testing Flow
1. Wazuh server (192.168.1.77) — ensure API accessible:
let token = null;
// Get JWT token
async function getToken() {
  const res = await axios.post(`${WAZUH_API}/security/user/authenticate`, {
    username: 'wazuh',
    password: 'wazuh'
  }, { httpsAgent: agent });
  token = res.data.data.token;
}
// Proxy endpoint for agents list
app.get('/api/agents', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    if (!token) await getToken();
    const response = await axios.get(`${WAZUH_API}/agents`, {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` },
      httpsAgent: agent
    });
    res.json(response.data);
  } catch (err) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
  }
});
app.listen(3001, () => console.log('Proxy running on http://localhost:3001'));
javascript
fetch('http://localhost:3001/api/agents')
  .then(res => res.json())
  .then(data => console.log(data));
Use Case Endpoint
Agents list GET /agents
Agent details GET /agents/:id
Alerts GET /manager/alerts
Syscheck GET /syscheck/:agent_id
SCA scan GET /sca/:agent_id
Stats GET /manager/stats/hourly
bash
curl -k -u wazuh:wazuh https://192.168.1.77:55000/agents

// Wazuh API Configuration
const WAZUH_API = 'https://192.168.1.77:55000';
const USERNAME = 'wazuh';
const PASSWORD = 'wazuh'; // Ya aapka actual password
let authToken = null;
// Get JWT Token
async function authenticate() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${WAZUH_API}/security/user/authenticate`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Authorization': 'Basic ' + btoa(`${USERNAME}:${PASSWORD}`)
            },
            // Certificate error ke liye (development only)
            mode: 'cors'
        });
        const data = await response.json();
        authToken = data.data.token;
        console.log('Authenticated successfully');
        return authToken;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Auth failed:', error);
    }
}
// Get Agents List
async function getAgents() {
    if (!authToken) await authenticate();

javascript
const express = require('express');
const axios = require('axios');
const https = require('https');
const cors = require('cors');
const app = express();
app.use(cors());
// Ignore self-signed certificate
const agent = new https.Agent({ rejectUnauthorized: false });
const WAZUH_URL = 'https://192.168.1.77:55000';
const CREDS = { username: 'wazuh', password: 'wazuh' };
let token = null;
// Auto-authenticate
async function getToken() {
    const res = await axios.post(`${WAZUH_URL}/security/user/authenticate`, 
        CREDS, { httpsAgent: agent });
    token = res.data.data.token;
    return token;
}
// Proxy routes
app.get('/api/agents', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        if (!token) await getToken();
        const response = await axios.get(`${WAZUH_URL}/agents`, {
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` },
            httpsAgent: agent
        });
        res.json(response.data);
    } catch (err) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
    }
});
// Add more endpoints as needed
app.get('/api/alerts', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        if (!token) await getToken();
        const response = await axios.get(`${WAZUH_URL}/manager/alerts`, {
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` },
            httpsAgent: agent
        });
        res.json(response.data);
    } catch (err) {

class Handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):        def do_GET(self):        parsed = urlparse(self.path)        self.send_response(200)        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')        self.end_headers()                if parsed.path == '/health':            resp = {"status": "ok"}        elif parsed.path == '/scan':            params = parse_qs(parsed.query)            resp = self.scan(params)        else:            resp = {"error": "Use /scan"}                self.wfile.write(json.dumps(resp).encode())        def scan(self, params):        min_level = int(params.get('min_level', ['1'])[0])        max_level = int(params.get('max_level', ['15'])[0])        start_date = params.get('start_date', [None])[0]        end_date = params.get('end_date', [None])[0]        event_id = params.get('event_id', [None])[0]        rule_id = params.get('rule_id', [None])[0]        description = params.get('description', [None])[0]        limit = min(int(params.get('limit', ['500'])[0]), 2000)                must = []        must.append({"range": {"rule.level": {"gte": min_level, "lte": max_level}}})                if start_date:            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"gte": self._parse_date(start_date)}}})        if end_date:            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"lte": self._parse_date(end_date)}}})                if event_id:            must.append({"term": {"data.win.system.eventID": event_id}})                # FIX: Use match for rule.id (it's a text field)        if rule_id:            must.append({"match": {"rule.id": rule_id}})                if description:            must.append({"match": {"rule.description": description}})                query_dict = {            "size": limit,            "sort": [{"timestamp": {"order": "desc"}}],            "query": {"bool": {"must": must}}        }                query_str = json.dumps(query_dict)        auth_str = base64.b64encode(f"{INDEXER_USER}:{INDEXER_PASS}".encode()).decode()                cmd = [            'curl', '-k', '-s',            '-H', f'Authorization: Basic {auth_str}',            '-H', 'Content-Type: application/json',

        proxy_pass http://127.0.0.1:9999;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        add_header 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin' '*';
        add_header 'Access-Control-Allow-Methods' 'GET, POST, OPTIONS';
    }
}
EOF

INDEXER_URL = "https://localhost:9200"INDEXER_USER = "admin"INDEXER_PASS = "bqUxnAP*Mw2b+qLaI2ansmKNlCqoCHs7"INDEX_PATTERN = "wazuh-alerts-4.x-*"
class Handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):        def do_GET(self):        parsed = urlparse(self.path)        self.send_response(200)        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')        self.end_headers()                if parsed.path == '/health':            resp = {"status": "ok"}        elif parsed.path == '/scan':            params = parse_qs(parsed.query)            resp = self.scan(params)        else:            resp = {"error": "Use /scan"}                self.wfile.write(json.dumps(resp).encode())        def scan(self, params):        min_level = int(params.get('min_level', ['1'])[0])        max_level = int(params.get('max_level', ['15'])[0])        start_date = params.get('start_date', [None])[0]        end_date = params.get('end_date', [None])[0]        event_id = params.get('event_id', [None])[0]        rule_id = params.get('rule_id', [None])[0]        description = params.get('description', [None])[0]        limit = min(int(params.get('limit', ['500'])[0]), 2000)                must = []        must.append({"range": {"rule.level": {"gte": min_level, "lte": max_level}}})                if start_date:            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"gte": self._parse_date(start_date)}}})        if end_date:

--- Page 27 ---
            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"lte": self._parse_date(end_date)}}})                if event_id:            must.append({"term": {"data.win.system.eventID": event_id}})                # FIX: Use match for rule.id (it's a text field)        if rule_id:            must.append({"match": {"rule.id": rule_id}})                if description:            must.append({"match": {"rule.description": description}})                query_dict = {            "size": limit,            "sort": [{"timestamp": {"order": "desc"}}],            "query": {"bool": {"must": must}}        }                query_str = json.dumps(query_dict)        auth_str = base64.b64encode(f"{INDEXER_USER}:{INDEXER_PASS}".encode()).decode()                cmd = [            'curl', '-k', '-s',            '-H', f'Authorization: Basic {auth_str}',            '-H', 'Content-Type: application/json',            '-X', 'POST',            f'{INDEXER_URL}/{INDEX_PATTERN}/_search',            '-d', query_str        ]                try:            result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)            data = json.loads(result.stdout)            total = data.get('hits', {}).get('total', {}).get('value', 0)            hits = data.get('hits', {}).get('hits', [])            raw_alerts = [hit['_source'] for hit in hits]            return {"success": True, "total": total, "count": len(raw_alerts), "results": raw_alerts}        except Exception as e:            return {"success": False, "error": str(e), "results": []}        def _parse_date(self, date_str):        formats = ['%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M', '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M', '%Y-%m-%d']        for fmt in formats:            try:                return datetime.strptime(date_str, fmt).strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S')            except:                continue        return date_str        def log_message(self, format, *args):        pass

javascript
// ==================== CONFIGURATION ====================
const API_BASE = 'http://192.168.1.77:9999';
let currentResults = [];
let autoRefreshTimer = null;
let isAutoRefresh = false;
// ==================== INITIALIZATION ====================
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    checkAPIHealth();
    updateRangeValues();
});
// ==================== API HEALTH CHECK ====================
async function checkAPIHealth() {
    const statusDot = document.querySelector('#api-status .dot');
    const statusText = document.querySelector('#api-status span:last-child');
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/health`);
        const data = await response.json();
        
        if (data.status === 'ok') {
            statusDot.classList.add('connected');
            statusText.textContent = 'API: Connected';
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 37/178

--- Page 38 ---
            document.getElementById('api-status').querySelector('span:last-child').style.
color = '#00c853';
        }
    } catch (error) {
        statusDot.classList.remove('connected');
        statusText.textContent = 'API: Disconnected';
        console.error('API Health Check Failed:', error);
    }
}
// ==================== RANGE SLIDERS ====================
function updateRangeValue(type) {
    const value = document.getElementById(`${type}-level`).value;
    document.getElementById(`${type}-value`).textContent = value;
    updateRangeValues();
}
function updateRangeValues() {
    const min = parseInt(document.getElementById('min-level').value);
    const max = parseInt(document.getElementById('max-level').value);
    
    document.getElementById('min-value').textContent = min;
    document.getElementById('max-value').textContent = max;
    
    // Color coding
    const minValueEl = document.getElementById('min-value');
    const maxValueEl = document.getElementById('max-value');
    
    minValueEl.style.background = getLevelColor(min);
    maxValueEl.style.background = getLevelColor(max);
}
function getLevelColor(level) {
    if (level >= 12) return '#ff1744';
    if (level >= 7) return '#ff9100';
    return '#00c853';
}
// ==================== SEARCH ALERTS ====================
async function searchAlerts() {
    showLoading(true);
    
    try {
        const params = buildQueryParams();
        const url = `${API_BASE}/scan?${params}`;
        
        console.log('Fetching:', url);
        
        const response = await fetch(url);
        const data = await response.json();
        
        if (data.success) {
            currentResults = data.results;
            updateStats(data);
            renderAlertsTable(data.results);
            updateQueryInfo(params);
            updateLastUpdateTime();
        } else {
            showError(data.error || 'Unknown error occurred');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Search failed:', error);
        showError('Failed to fetch alerts. Check API connection.');
        document.getElementById('api-status').querySelector('.dot').classList.remove('con
nected');
    } finally {
        showLoading(false);
    }
}
function buildQueryParams() {
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 38/178

--- Page 39 ---
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    
    // Level range
    params.append('min_level', document.getElementById('min-level').value);
    params.append('max_level', document.getElementById('max-level').value);
    
    // Rule ID
    const ruleId = document.getElementById('rule-id').value.trim();
    if (ruleId) params.append('rule_id', ruleId);
    
    // Event ID
    const eventId = document.getElementById('event-id').value.trim();
    if (eventId) params.append('event_id', eventId);
    
    // Description
    const description = document.getElementById('description').value.trim();
    if (description) params.append('description', description);
    
    // Dates
    const startDate = document.getElementById('start-date').value;
    if (startDate) params.append('start_date', startDate);
    
    const endDate = document.getElementById('end-date').value;
    if (endDate) params.append('end_date', endDate);
    
    // Limit
    params.append('limit', document.getElementById('limit').value);
    
    return params.toString();
}
// ==================== UPDATE STATS ====================
function updateStats(data) {
    document.getElementById('total-count').textContent = data.total;
    
    const critical = data.results.filter(a => a.rule.level >= 12).length;
    const warning = data.results.filter(a => a.rule.level >= 7 && a.rule.level <= 11).len
gth;
    const info = data.results.filter(a => a.rule.level < 7).length;
    
    document.getElementById('critical-count').textContent = critical;
    document.getElementById('warning-count').textContent = warning;
    document.getElementById('info-count').textContent = info;
}
// ==================== RENDER ALERTS TABLE ====================
function renderAlertsTable(alerts) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('alerts-tbody');
    
    if (!alerts || alerts.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="7" class="no-data">No alerts found matching y
our criteria</td></tr>';
        return;
    }
    
    tbody.innerHTML = alerts.map((alert, index) => {
        const timestamp = alert.timestamp || 'N/A';
        const level = alert.rule?.level || 0;
        const ruleId = alert.rule?.id || 'N/A';
        const description = alert.rule?.description || 'No description';
        const agent = alert.agent?.name || 'N/A';
        const sourceIp = alert.data?.srcip || 'N/A';
        
        const levelClass = level >= 12 ? 'level-critical' : 
                          level >= 7 ? 'level-warning' : 'level-info';
        
        return `
            <tr>
                <td>${formatTimestamp(timestamp)}</td>
                <td><span class="level-badge ${levelClass}">${level}</span></td>
                <td>${ruleId}</td>
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 39/178

--- Page 40 ---
                <td title="${description}">${truncate(description, 60)}</td>
                <td>${agent}</td>
                <td>${sourceIp}</td>
                <td><button class="view-btn" onclick="viewDetails(${index})">Details</but
ton></td>
            </tr>
        `;
    }).join('');
}
function formatTimestamp(timestamp) {
    if (!timestamp || timestamp === 'N/A') return 'N/A';
    try {
        const date = new Date(timestamp);
        return date.toLocaleString();
    } catch {
        return timestamp;
    }
}
function truncate(text, maxLength) {
    if (!text) return '';
    return text.length > maxLength ? text.substring(0, maxLength) + '...' : text;
}
// ==================== VIEW DETAILS ====================
function viewDetails(index) {
    const alert = currentResults[index];
    const modal = document.getElementById('alert-modal');
    const detailPre = document.getElementById('alert-detail');
    
    detailPre.textContent = JSON.stringify(alert, null, 2);
    modal.style.display = 'block';
}
function closeModal() {
    document.getElementById('alert-modal').style.display = 'none';
}
// Close modal on outside click
window.onclick = function(event) {
    const modal = document.getElementById('alert-modal');
    if (event.target === modal) {
        modal.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

// ==================== EXPORT TO CSV ====================
function exportToCSV() {
    if (!currentResults || currentResults.length === 0) {
        alert('No data to export!');
        return;
    }
    
    const headers = ['Timestamp', 'Level', 'Rule ID', 'Description', 'Agent', 'Source I
P', 'Event ID'];
    const rows = currentResults.map(alert => [
        alert.timestamp || '',
        alert.rule?.level || '',
        alert.rule?.id || '',
        `"${(alert.rule?.description || '').replace(/"/g, '""')}"`,
        alert.agent?.name || '',
        alert.data?.srcip || '',
        alert.data?.win?.system?.eventID || ''
    ]);
    
    const csv = [headers.join(','), ...rows.map(row => row.join(','))].join('\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    
    a.href = url;
    a.download = `wazuh-alerts-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)}.csv`;
    a.click();
    
    window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);

    def do_OPTIONS(self):
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type')
        self.end_headers()
    
    # ==================== ELASTICSEARCH QUERY HELPER ====================
    def es_query(self, method, path, body=None):
        auth_str = base64.b64encode(f"{INDEXER_USER}:{INDEXER_PASS}".encode()).decode()
        cmd = ['curl', '-k', '-s', '-X', method,
               '-H', f'Authorization: Basic {auth_str}',
               '-H', 'Content-Type: application/json',
               f'{INDEXER_URL}{path}']
        if body:
            cmd.extend(['-d', json.dumps(body)])
        
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)
            return json.loads(result.stdout)
        except Exception as e:
            return {"error": str(e)}
    
    # ==================== GET ALL INDICES ====================
    def get_indices(self):
        data = self.es_query('GET', '/_cat/indices?format=json&bytes=b')
        if 'error' in data:
            return data
        
        indices = []
        for idx in data:
            name = idx.get('index', '')
            if name.startswith('.'):
                continue

        patterns = {}

            pattern = idx['pattern']
            if pattern not in patterns:
                patterns[pattern] = {
                    "pattern": pattern,
                    "indices": [],
                    "total_docs": 0,
                    "total_size": "0",
                    "count": 0
                }
            patterns[pattern]['indices'].append(idx)
            patterns[pattern]['total_docs'] += idx['docs_count']
            patterns[pattern]['count'] += 1
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "total_indices": len(indices),
            "patterns": list(patterns.values()),
            "all_indices": sorted([idx['name'] for idx in indices], reverse=True)
        }
    
    def _extract_pattern(self, name):
        parts = name.split('-')
        if len(parts) >= 3:
            if parts[2].startswith('20'):  # Date pattern
                return '-'.join(parts[:2]) + '-*'
        if len(parts) >= 2:
            return parts[0] + '-*'
        return name + '*'
    
    # ==================== GET INDEX STATS ====================
    def get_index_stats(self, index_name):
        data = self.es_query('GET', f'/{index_name}/_stats')
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": data['error']}
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "index": index_name,
            "docs_count": data.get('_all', {}).get('total', {}).get('docs', {}).get('coun
t', 0),
            "size_bytes": data.get('_all', {}).get('total', {}).get('store', {}).get('siz
e_in_bytes', 0)
        }

    # ==================== SCAN ALERTS (ORIGINAL) ====================
    def scan_alerts(self, params):
        min_level = int(params.get('min_level', ['1'])[0])
        max_level = int(params.get('max_level', ['15'])[0])
        start_date = params.get('start_date', [None])[0]
        end_date = params.get('end_date', [None])[0]
        event_id = params.get('event_id', [None])[0]
        rule_id = params.get('rule_id', [None])[0]
        description = params.get('description', [None])[0]
        limit = min(int(params.get('limit', ['500'])[0]), 2000)
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        
        must = []
        must.append({"range": {"rule.level": {"gte": min_level, "lte": max_level}}})
        
        if start_date:
            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"gte": self._parse_date(start_date)}}})
        if end_date:
            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"lte": self._parse_date(end_date)}}})
        if event_id:
            must.append({"term": {"data.win.system.eventID": event_id}})
        if rule_id:
            must.append({"match": {"rule.id": rule_id}})
        if description:
            must.append({"match": {"rule.description": description}})
        
        query_dict = {
            "size": limit,
            "sort": [{"timestamp": {"order": "desc"}}],
            "query": {"bool": {"must": must}}
        }
        
        data = self.es_query('POST', f'/{index_pattern}/_search', query_dict)
        
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": str(data['error'])}
        
        total = data.get('hits', {}).get('total', {}).get('value', 0)
        hits = data.get('hits', {}).get('hits', [])
        raw_alerts = []
        for hit in hits:
            alert = hit['_source']
            alert['_id'] = hit.get('_id', '')
            alert['_index'] = hit.get('_index', '')
            raw_alerts.append(alert)
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "total": total,
            "count": len(raw_alerts),
            "results": raw_alerts
        }
    
    # ==================== SEARCH DOCUMENTS (NEW) ====================
    def search_documents(self, params):

ND"}})

    # ==================== COUNT DOCUMENTS ====================
    def count_documents(self, params):
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        query_text = params.get('q', [''])[0]
        
        query_dict = {"query": {"query_string": {"query": query_text}}} if query_text els
e {"query": {"match_all": {}}}
        data = self.es_query('POST', f'/{index_pattern}/_count', query_dict)
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "index": index_pattern,
            "count": data.get('count', 0)
        }
    
    def _parse_date(self, date_str):
        if not date_str:
            return None
        formats = ['%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M', '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M', '%Y-%m-%d', '%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S']
        for fmt in formats:
            try:
                return datetime.strptime(date_str, fmt).strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S')
            except:
                continue
        return date_str
    
    def log_message(self, format, *args):
        pass

    print(f"Endpoints: /health, /indices, /scan, /search, /count, /fields")
    HTTPServer(('0.0.0.0', PORT), Handler).serve_forever()

const API_BASE = 'http://192.168.1.77:9999';
let allIndices = [];
let currentIndexPattern = '';
let currentPage = 1;
let pageSize = 50;
let totalHits = 0;
let totalPages = 1;

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    checkHealth();
    loadIndices();
    updateTimeButtons('all');

// ==================== API HEALTH CHECK ====================
async function checkHealth() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/health`);
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.status === 'ok') {
            document.querySelector('.status-dot').classList.add('connected');
            document.getElementById('status-text').textContent = 'Connected';
        }
    } catch (e) {
        document.querySelector('.status-dot').classList.remove('connected');
        document.getElementById('status-text').textContent = 'Disconnected';
    }
}
// ==================== LOAD INDICES ====================
async function loadIndices() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/indices`);
        const data = await res.json();
        
        if (data.success) {
            allIndices = data.all_indices || [];
            renderIndexDropdown(data.patterns || []);
            renderSidebarIndices(data.patterns || []);
            updateSidebarStats(data);
        }
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek

    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Failed to load indices:', e);
    }

function renderIndexDropdown(patterns) {
    const select = document.getElementById('index-pattern');
    select.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select Index Pattern --</option>';
    
    patterns.forEach(p => {
        const option = document.createElement('option');
        option.value = p.pattern;
        option.textContent = `${p.pattern} (${p.total_docs.toLocaleString()} docs, ${p.co
unt} indices)`;
        select.appendChild(option);
    });
    
    // Add individual indices
    patterns.forEach(p => {
        p.indices.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(idx => {
            const option = document.createElement('option');
            option.value = idx.name;
            option.textContent = `  └─ ${idx.name} (${idx.docs_count.toLocaleString()} do
cs)`;
            option.style.fontSize = '12px';
            option.style.color = '#888';
            select.appendChild(option);
        });
    });
    
    select.onchange = function() {
        currentIndexPattern = this.value;
        if (currentIndexPattern) {
            currentPage = 1;
            executeSearch();
        }
    };
}
function renderSidebarIndices(patterns) {
    const container = document.getElementById('indices-list');
    let html = '';
    
    patterns.forEach(p => {
        html += `
            <div style="padding: 8px 15px; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12px; color: var
(--accent); background: var(--bg-dark);">
                📁  ${p.pattern} (${p.count})
            </div>
        `;
        
        p.indices.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(idx => {
            const healthClass = idx.health === 'green' ? 'health-green' : 
                               idx.health === 'yellow' ? 'health-yellow' : 'health-red';
            html += `
                <div class="index-item ${idx.name === currentIndexPattern ? 'selected' : 
''}" 
                     onclick="selectIndexFromSidebar('${idx.name}')" 
                     title="${idx.name}">
                    <div>
                        <span class="index-health ${healthClass}">●</span>
                        <span class="index-name">${idx.name.split('-').pop()}</span>
                    </div>
                    <span class="index-count">${idx.docs_count.toLocaleString()}</span>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    });
    
    container.innerHTML = html || '<div class="loading-text">No indices found</div>';
}

function selectIndexFromSidebar(indexName) {
    currentIndexPattern = indexName;
    document.getElementById('index-pattern').value = indexName;
    currentPage = 1;
    executeSearch();
    renderSidebarIndices(getPatternsFromCache());
}
function updateSidebarStats(data) {
    document.getElementById('total-indices').textContent = data.total_indices || 0;
    let totalDocs = 0;
    (data.patterns || []).forEach(p => totalDocs += p.total_docs);
    document.getElementById('total-docs').textContent = totalDocs.toLocaleString();
}

    // Simplified - returns empty array if not needed

function filterSidebarIndices() {
    const filter = document.getElementById('sidebar-filter').value.toLowerCase();
    const items = document.querySelectorAll('.index-item');
    items.forEach(item => {
        const text = item.textContent.toLowerCase();
        item.style.display = text.includes(filter) ? 'flex' : 'none';
    });
}
// ==================== EXECUTE SEARCH ====================
async function executeSearch() {
    if (!currentIndexPattern) {
        alert('Please select an index pattern first!');
        return;
    }
    
    showLoading(true);
    searchStartTime = Date.now();
    
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    params.append('index', currentIndexPattern);
    params.append('limit', pageSize);
    params.append('offset', (currentPage - 1) * pageSize);
    params.append('sort', currentSortField);
    params.append('order', currentSortOrder);
    
    const queryText = document.getElementById('search-input').value.trim();
    if (queryText) params.append('q', queryText);
    
    // Advanced filters
    const ruleMin = document.getElementById('filter-rule-min').value;
    if (ruleMin) params.append('rule_level_min', ruleMin);
    
    const ruleMax = document.getElementById('filter-rule-max').value;
    if (ruleMax) params.append('rule_level_max', ruleMax);
    
    const ruleId = document.getElementById('filter-rule-id').value.trim();
    if (ruleId) params.append('rule_id', ruleId);
    
    const agent = document.getElementById('filter-agent').value.trim();
    if (agent) params.append('agent_name', agent);
    
    // Date filters
    const activeTimeBtn = document.querySelector('.time-btn.active');
    if (activeTimeBtn && activeTimeBtn.dataset.range && activeTimeBtn.dataset.range !== 
'all') {
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 65/178

--- Page 66 ---
        params.append('start_date', getTimeRangeStart(activeTimeBtn.dataset.range));
    }
    
    const customStart = document.getElementById('custom-start').value;
    if (customStart) params.append('start_date', customStart);
    
    const customEnd = document.getElementById('custom-end').value;
    if (customEnd) params.append('end_date', customEnd);
    
    try {
        const url = `${API_BASE}/search?${params.toString()}`;
        console.log('Search URL:', url);
        
        const res = await fetch(url);
        const data = await res.json();
        
        if (data.success) {
            currentResults = data.results;
            totalHits = data.total;
            totalPages = Math.ceil(totalHits / pageSize);
            renderTable(currentResults);
            updateResultsInfo(data);
            updatePagination();
        } else {
            alert('Search error: ' + (data.error || 'Unknown error'));
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Search failed:', e);
        alert('Failed to connect to API');
    } finally {
        showLoading(false);
    }
}
// ==================== RENDER TABLE ====================
function renderTable(results) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('table-body');
    
    if (!results || results.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = `
            <tr>
                <td colspan="7" class="empty-state">
                    <div class="empty-icon"> 📭 </div>
                    <h3>No documents found</h3>
                    <p>Try adjusting your search criteria or selecting a different index
</p>
                </td>
            </tr>
        `;
        return;
    }
    
    tbody.innerHTML = results.map((doc, i) => {
        const timestamp = doc.timestamp || '';
        const level = doc.rule?.level || 0;
        const ruleId = doc.rule?.id || '';
        const description = doc.rule?.description || '';
        const agent = doc.agent?.name || '';
        const index = doc._index || '';
        
        let levelClass = 'level-low';
        if (level >= 12) levelClass = 'level-critical';
        else if (level >= 7) levelClass = 'level-high';
        else if (level >= 4) levelClass = 'level-medium';
        
        return `
            <tr onclick="viewDocument(${i})" class="clickable-row">
                <td class="col-index" title="${index}">${index.split('-').pop()}</td>
                <td class="col-time">${formatTimestamp(timestamp)}</td>
                <td class="col-level"><span class="level-badge ${levelClass}">${level}</s
pan></td>
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek

--- Page 67 ---
                <td class="col-rule">${ruleId}</td>
                <td class="col-agent">${agent}</td>
                <td class="col-desc" title="${escapeHtml(description)}">${escapeHtml(desc
ription).substring(0, 80)}</td>
                <td class="col-actions">
                    <button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); viewDocu
ment(${i})"> 👁 </button>
                </td>
            </tr>
        `;
    }).join('');
}
function formatTimestamp(ts) {
    if (!ts) return 'N/A';
    try {
        const d = new Date(ts);
        return d.toLocaleString();
    } catch { return ts; }
}
function escapeHtml(text) {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = text;
    return div.innerHTML;
}
// ==================== VIEW DOCUMENT DETAIL ====================
function viewDocument(index) {
    const doc = currentResults[index];
    if (!doc) return;
    
    // Table view
    const detailTable = document.querySelector('#detail-table tbody');
    detailTable.innerHTML = '';
    
    const flattenObject = (obj, prefix = '') => {
        const rows = [];
        for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
            const fullKey = prefix ? `${prefix}.${key}` : key;
            if (value && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
                rows.push(...flattenObject(value, fullKey));
            } else {
                rows.push({ key: fullKey, value: value });
            }
        }
        return rows;
    };
    
    const flatData = flattenObject(doc);
    flatData.forEach(row => {
        const tr = document.createElement('tr');
        tr.innerHTML = `
            <td>${row.key}</td>
            <td>${typeof row.value === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(row.value) : row.value}
</td>
        `;
        detailTable.appendChild(tr);
    });
    
    // JSON view
    document.getElementById('detail-json').textContent = JSON.stringify(doc, null, 2);
    
    document.getElementById('detail-modal').classList.add('show');
    switchTab('table');
}
function closeDetailModal() {
    document.getElementById('detail-modal').classList.remove('show');
}

function switchTab(tab) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    event.target.classList.add('active');
    
    document.getElementById('detail-table-view').style.display = tab === 'table' ? 'bloc
k' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('detail-json-view').style.display = tab === 'json' ? 'block' 
: 'none';
}
// ==================== PAGINATION ====================
function updatePagination() {
    document.getElementById('page-info').textContent = `Page ${currentPage} of ${totalPag
es || 1}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-first').disabled = currentPage <= 1;
    document.getElementById('btn-prev').disabled = currentPage <= 1;
    document.getElementById('btn-next').disabled = currentPage >= totalPages;
    document.getElementById('btn-last').disabled = currentPage >= totalPages;
    document.getElementById('goto-page').value = currentPage;
    document.getElementById('goto-page').max = totalPages;
}
function goToPage(page) {
    if (page < 1 || page > totalPages) return;
    currentPage = page;
    executeSearch();
}
function nextPage() {
    if (currentPage < totalPages) {
        currentPage++;
        executeSearch();
    }
}
function previousPage() {
    if (currentPage > 1) {
        currentPage--;
        executeSearch();
    }
}
function changePageSize() {
    pageSize = parseInt(document.getElementById('rows-per-page').value);
    currentPage = 1;
    executeSearch();
}
// ==================== SORTING ====================
function sortTable(field) {
    if (currentSortField === field) {
        currentSortOrder = currentSortOrder === 'desc' ? 'asc' : 'desc';
    } else {
        currentSortField = field;
        currentSortOrder = 'desc';
    }
    executeSearch();
}

        document.getElementById('custom-end').value = '';
    } else {
        document.getElementById('custom-start').value = getTimeRangeStart(range);
        document.getElementById('custom-end').value = '';
    }
    if (currentIndexPattern) {
        currentPage = 1;

function updateTimeButtons(activeRange) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.time-btn').forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.remove('active');
        if (btn.textContent.toLowerCase().replace(' ', '') === activeRange || 
            (activeRange === 'all' && btn.textContent === 'All')) {
            btn.classList.add('active');
        }
    });
}
function getTimeRangeStart(range) {
    const now = new Date();
    switch(range) {
        case '15m': return new Date(now - 15*60000).toISOString().slice(0,16);
        case '1h': return new Date(now - 3600000).toISOString().slice(0,16);
        case '24h': return new Date(now - 86400000).toISOString().slice(0,16);
        case '7d': return new Date(now - 7*86400000).toISOString().slice(0,16);
        case '30d': return new Date(now - 30*86400000).toISOString().slice(0,16);
        default: return '';
    }
}

function exportCSV() {
    if (!currentResults.length) return alert('No data to export!');
    
    const headers = ['Index', 'Timestamp', 'Level', 'Rule ID', 'Description', 'Agent', 'S
ource IP'];
    const rows = currentResults.map(doc => [
        doc._index || '',
        doc.timestamp || '',
        doc.rule?.level || '',
        doc.rule?.id || '',
        `"${(doc.rule?.description || '').replace(/"/g, '""')}"`,
        doc.agent?.name || '',
        doc.data?.srcip || ''
    ]);
    
    const csv = [headers.join(','), ...rows.map(r => r.join(','))].join('\n');
    downloadFile(csv, `wazuh-export-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.csv`, 'text/c
sv');
}
function exportJSON() {
    if (!currentResults.length) return alert('No data to export!');
    downloadFile(JSON.stringify(currentResults, null, 2), 
                `wazuh-export-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.json`, 
                'application/json');
}
function downloadFile(content, filename, type) {
    const blob = new Blob([content], { type });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = filename;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

    if (e.target === this) closeDetailModal();
});

// ==================== CONFIGURATION ====================
const API_BASE = 'http://192.168.1.77:9999';
let allIndices = [];
let currentIndexPattern = '';
let currentPage = 1;

let totalHits = 0;
let totalPages = 1;

let currentSortOrder = 'desc';

// Column Management
let availableFields = [];
let selectedColumns = [];
const defaultColumns = [
    { name: '_index', label: 'Index', width: '150px' },
    { name: 'timestamp', label: 'Time', width: '170px' },
    { name: 'rule.level', label: 'Level', width: '70px' },
    { name: 'rule.id', label: 'Rule', width: '100px' },

// ==================== LOAD/SAVE SETTINGS ====================
function loadSavedSettings() {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('wazuh-dashboard-settings');
    if (saved) {
        try {
            const settings = JSON.parse(saved);
            selectedColumns = settings.selectedColumns || [...defaultColumns];
            pageSize = settings.pageSize || 50;
            refreshSeconds = settings.refreshSeconds || 0;
            currentSortField = settings.sortField || 'timestamp';
            currentSortOrder = settings.sortOrder || 'desc';
            
            if (refreshSeconds > 0) {
                startAutoRefresh(refreshSeconds);
                updateRefreshButtons(refreshSeconds);
            }
            if (settings.indexPattern) {
                currentIndexPattern = settings.indexPattern;
                setTimeout(() => {
                    document.getElementById('index-pattern').value = currentIndexPattern;
                }, 500);
            }
        } catch(e) {
            selectedColumns = [...defaultColumns];
        }
    } else {
        selectedColumns = [...defaultColumns];
    }
}
function saveSettings() {
    const settings = {
        selectedColumns,

https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 80/178

        pageSize,
        refreshSeconds,
        sortField: currentSortField,
        sortOrder: currentSortOrder,
        indexPattern: currentIndexPattern
    };
    localStorage.setItem('wazuh-dashboard-settings', JSON.stringify(settings));
}
// ==================== API HEALTH CHECK ====================
async function checkHealth() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/health`);
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.status === 'ok') {
            document.querySelector('.status-dot').classList.add('connected');
            document.getElementById('status-text').textContent = 'Connected';
        }
    } catch (e) {
        document.querySelector('.status-dot').classList.remove('connected');
        document.getElementById('status-text').textContent = 'Disconnected';
    }
}
// ==================== LOAD INDICES ====================
async function loadIndices() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/indices`);
        const data = await res.json();
        
        if (data.success) {
            allIndices = data.all_indices || [];
            renderIndexDropdown(data.patterns || []);
            renderSidebarIndices(data.patterns || []);
            updateSidebarStats(data);
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Failed to load indices:', e);
    }
}
function renderIndexDropdown(patterns) {
    const select = document.getElementById('index-pattern');
    select.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select Index Pattern --</option>';
    
    patterns.forEach(p => {
        const option = document.createElement('option');
        option.value = p.pattern;
        option.textContent = `${p.pattern} (${p.total_docs.toLocaleString()} docs)`;
        select.appendChild(option);
        
        p.indices.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(idx => {
            const sub = document.createElement('option');
            sub.value = idx.name;
            sub.textContent = `  └─ ${idx.name}`;
            sub.style.fontSize = '11px';
            select.appendChild(sub);
        });
    });
    
    select.onchange = function() {
        currentIndexPattern = this.value;
        if (currentIndexPattern) {
            currentPage = 1;
            executeSearch();
            saveSettings();
        }
    };
}

function updateSidebarStats(data) {
    document.getElementById('total-indices').textContent = data.total_indices || 0;
    let td = 0;

}

function filterSidebarIndices() {

e';
    });
}
// ==================== SETTINGS PANEL ====================
function openSettings() {
    document.getElementById('settings-panel').classList.add('open');
    document.getElementById('settings-overlay').classList.add('show');
    renderColumnManager();

}
function closeSettings() {
    document.getElementById('settings-panel').classList.remove('open');
    document.getElementById('settings-overlay').classList.remove('show');
    saveSettings();
}
// ==================== AUTO REFRESH ====================
function setRefreshInterval(seconds) {
    refreshSeconds = seconds;
    updateRefreshButtons(seconds);
    
    if (autoRefreshInterval) clearInterval(autoRefreshInterval);
    if (countdownTimer) clearInterval(countdownTimer);
    
    if (seconds > 0) {
        startAutoRefresh(seconds);
        showToast(`Auto-refresh set to ${formatSeconds(seconds)}`, 'success');
    } else {
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 82/178

        document.getElementById('refresh-status').innerHTML = 'Auto-refresh: <strong>OFF
</strong>';
        showToast('Auto-refresh disabled', 'info');
    }
    saveSettings();
}
function setCustomRefresh() {
    const value = parseInt(document.getElementById('custom-refresh-value').value);
    const unit = parseInt(document.getElementById('custom-refresh-unit').value);
    const seconds = value * unit;
    if (seconds > 0) setRefreshInterval(seconds);
}
function startAutoRefresh(seconds) {
    if (autoRefreshInterval) clearInterval(autoRefreshInterval);
    if (countdownTimer) clearInterval(countdownTimer);
    
    let remaining = seconds;
    updateCountdown(remaining);
    
    countdownTimer = setInterval(() => {
        remaining--;
        updateCountdown(remaining);
    }, 1000);
    
    autoRefreshInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (currentIndexPattern) executeSearch(true);
        remaining = seconds;
        updateCountdown(remaining);
    }, seconds * 1000);
    
    document.getElementById('refresh-status').innerHTML = 
        `Auto-refresh: <strong>${formatSeconds(seconds)}</strong> | Next in: <span class
="countdown">${formatSeconds(remaining)}</span>`;
}
function updateCountdown(remaining) {
    document.getElementById('refresh-status').innerHTML = 
        `Auto-refresh: <strong>${formatSeconds(refreshSeconds)}</strong> | Next in: <span 
class="countdown">${formatSeconds(remaining)}</span>`;
}
function updateRefreshButtons(activeSeconds) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.refresh-btn').forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.remove('active');
        if (parseInt(btn.dataset.interval) === activeSeconds) btn.classList.add('activ
e');
    });
}
function formatSeconds(s) {
    if (s < 60) return `${s}s`;
    const m = Math.floor(s / 60);
    const sec = s % 60;
    return sec > 0 ? `${m}m ${sec}s` : `${m}m`;
}
function toggleAutoRefresh() {
    if (refreshSeconds > 0) {
        setRefreshInterval(0);
    } else {
        setRefreshInterval(30); // Default 30s
    }
}
// ==================== COLUMN MANAGER ====================
async function renderColumnManager() {
    // Fetch fields if not loaded
    if (availableFields.length === 0 && currentIndexPattern) {
        await loadFields();
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 83/178

--- Page 84 ---
    }
    
    renderAvailableFields();
    renderSelectedColumns();
}
async function loadFields() {
    if (!currentIndexPattern) return;
    
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/fields?index=${currentIndexPattern}`);
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.success && data.fields) {
            availableFields = data.fields;
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.error('Failed to load fields:', e);
    }
}
function renderAvailableFields() {
    const container = document.getElementById('available-fields-list');
    const search = (document.getElementById('field-search')?.value || '').toLowerCase();
    
    const selectedNames = new Set(selectedColumns.map(c => c.name));
    const filtered = availableFields.filter(f => 
        f.name.toLowerCase().includes(search) && !selectedNames.has(f.name)
    );
    
    container.innerHTML = filtered.slice(0, 100).map(f => `
        <div class="field-item" onclick="addColumn('${f.name}', '${f.name.split('.').pop
()}')">
            <span class="field-name">${f.name}</span>
            <span>
                <span class="field-type">${f.type}</span>
                <button class="add-btn">+</button>
            </span>
        </div>
    `).join('');
}
function renderSelectedColumns() {
    const container = document.getElementById('selected-columns-list');
    
    container.innerHTML = selectedColumns.map((col, i) => `
        <div class="field-item selected" draggable="true" 
             ondragstart="dragStart(event, ${i})" 
             ondragover="dragOver(event)" 
             ondrop="drop(event, ${i})">
            <span class="drag-handle"> ⋮⋮ </span>
            <span class="field-name">${col.name}</span>
            <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeColumn(${i})">×</button>
        </div>
    `).join('');
    
    updateQuickColumnBar();
}
function addColumn(fieldName, label) {
    if (selectedColumns.find(c => c.name === fieldName)) return;
    selectedColumns.push({ name: fieldName, label: label || fieldName.split('.').pop(), w
idth: '150px' });
    renderColumnManager();
    executeSearch(true);
    saveSettings();
    showToast(`Added column: ${fieldName}`, 'success');
}
function removeColumn(index) {
    if (selectedColumns.length <= 2) {
        showToast('At least 2 columns required!', 'warning');

// Drag & Drop reorder
let draggedIndex = null;
function dragStart(e, index) {
    draggedIndex = index;
    e.target.classList.add('dragging');
}
function dragOver(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
}
function drop(e, targetIndex) {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (draggedIndex === null || draggedIndex === targetIndex) return;
    
    const [moved] = selectedColumns.splice(draggedIndex, 1);
    selectedColumns.splice(targetIndex, 0, moved);
    draggedIndex = null;
    
    renderColumnManager();
    executeSearch(true);
    saveSettings();
}
function updateQuickColumnBar() {
    const container = document.getElementById('column-badges');
    container.innerHTML = selectedColumns.map((col, i) => `
        <span class="column-badge" title="${col.name}">
            ${col.label}
            <span class="remove-col" onclick="event.stopPropagation();removeColumn
(${i})">×</span>
        </span>
    `).join('');
}

    openSettings();
    // Scroll to column manager section
    setTimeout(() => {
        document.querySelector('.settings-section:nth-child(2)')?.scrollIntoView({ behavi
or: 'smooth' });
    }, 300);
}

    selectedColumns = [...defaultColumns];
    renderColumnManager();
    executeSearch(true);
    saveSettings();
    showToast('Columns reset to default', 'info');
}

// ==================== EXECUTE SEARCH ====================
async function executeSearch(silent = false) {
    if (!currentIndexPattern) {
        if (!silent) alert('Please select an index pattern first!');
        return;
    }
    
    if (!silent) showLoading(true);
    searchStartTime = Date.now();
    
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    params.append('index', currentIndexPattern);
    params.append('lim

--- Page 87 ---
    const ruleMin = document.getElementById('filter-rule-min').value;
    if (ruleMin) params.append('rule_level_min', ruleMin);
    const ruleMax = document.getElementById('filter-rule-max').value;
    if (ruleMax) params.append('rule_level_max', ruleMax);
    const ruleId = document.getElementById('filter-rule-id').value.trim();
    if (ruleId) params.append('rule_id', ruleId);
    const agent = document.getElementById('filter-agent').value.trim();
    if (agent) params.append('agent_name', agent);
    
    const activeBtn = document.querySelector('.time-btn.active');
    if (activeBtn?.dataset.range && activeBtn.dataset.range !== 'all') {
        params.append('start_date', getTimeRangeStart(activeBtn.dataset.range));
    }
    const cs = document.getElementById('custom-start').value;
    if (cs) params.append('start_date', cs);
    const ce = document.getElementById('custom-end').value;
    if (ce) params.append('end_date', ce);
    
    try {
        const url = `${API_BASE}/search?${params.toString()}`;
        const res = await fetch(url);
        const data = await res.json();
        
        if (data.success) {
            currentResults = data.results;
            totalHits = data.total;
            totalPages = Math.ceil(totalHits / pageSize) || 1;
            renderTable(currentResults);
            updateResultsInfo(data);
            updatePagination();
            
            // Load fields for column manager
            if (availableFields.length === 0) loadFields();
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Search failed:', e);
        if (!silent) alert('Failed to connect to API');
    } finally {
        if (!silent) showLoading(false);
    }
}
// ==================== RENDER TABLE WITH DYNAMIC COLUMNS ====================
function renderTable(results) {
    const thead = document.getElementById('table-head');
    const tbody = document.getElementById('table-body');
    
    // Render header
    thead.innerHTML = '<tr>' + selectedColumns.map(col => 
        `<th style="width:${col.width};cursor:pointer;" onclick="sortTable('${col.nam
e}')" title="Sort by ${col.name}">
            ${col.label} ${currentSortField===col.name ? (currentSortOrder==='des
c'?'▼':'▲') : ' ⬍ '}
        </th>`
    ).join('') + '<th style="width:60px;"> 📋 </th></tr>';
    
    if (!results || results.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="${selectedColumns.length+1}" class="empty-sta
te">
            <div class="empty-icon"> 📭 </div><h3>No documents found</h3></td></tr>`;
        return;
    }
    
    tbody.innerHTML = results.map((doc, i) => {
        let rowHtml = '<tr onclick="viewDocument(' + i + ')" class="clickable-row">';
        
        selectedColumns.forEach(col => {
            const value = getNestedValue(doc, col.name);
            const display = formatCellValue(value, col.name);
            rowHtml += `<td title="${escapeHtml(String(value||''))}">${display}</td>`;
        });
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working ne

--- Page 88 ---
        
        rowHtml += '<td><button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="event.stopPropagation();viewD
ocument(' + i + ')"> 👁 </button></td>';
        rowHtml += '</tr>';
        return rowHtml;
    }).join('');
}
function getNestedValue(obj, path) {
    return path.split('.').reduce((current, key) => 
        current && current[key] !== undefined ? current[key] : null, obj);
}
function formatCellValue(value, fieldName) {
    if (value === null || value === undefined) return '<span style="color:#666;">-</span
>';
    
    // Special formatting
    if (fieldName === 'rule.level') {
        const level = parseInt(value);
        let cls = 'level-low';
        if (level >= 12) cls = 'level-critical';
        else if (level >= 7) cls = 'level-high';
        else if (level >= 4) cls = 'level-medium';
        return `<span class="level-badge ${cls}">${level}</span>`;
    }
    
    if (fieldName === 'timestamp') return formatTimestamp(value);
    
    if (typeof value === 'object') return JSON.stringify(value).substring(0, 50);
    
    return escapeHtml(String(value)).substring(0, 100);
}
function formatTimestamp(ts) {
    if (!ts) return 'N/A';
    try { return new Date(ts).toLocaleString(); }
    catch { return ts; }
}
function escapeHtml(text) {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = text;
    return div.innerHTML;
}
// ==================== PAGINATION & SORTING ====================
function updatePagination() {
    document.getElementById('page-info').textContent = `Page ${currentPage} of ${totalPag
es}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-first').disabled = currentPage <= 1;
    document.getElementById('btn-prev').disabled = currentPage <= 1;
    document.getElementById('btn-next').disabled = currentPage >= totalPages;
    document.getElementById('btn-last').disabled = currentPage >= totalPages;
    document.getElementById('goto-page').value = currentPage;
    document.getElementById('goto-page').max = totalPages;
}
function goToPage(page) {
    if (page < 1 || page > totalPages) return;
    currentPage = page;
    executeSearch();
}
function nextPage() { if (currentPage < totalPages) { currentPage++; executeSearch(); } }
function previousPage() { if (currentPage > 1) { currentPage--; executeSearch(); } }
function changePageSize() {
    pageSize = parseInt(document.getElementById('rows-per-page').value);
    currentPage = 1;
    executeSearch();

function sortTable(field) {
    if (currentSortField === field) {
        currentSortOrder = currentSortOrder === 'desc' ? 'asc' : 'desc';
    } else {
        currentSortField = field;
        currentSortOrder = 'desc';
    }
    executeSearch();
    saveSettings();
}
// ==================== DOCUMENT DETAIL ====================
function viewDocument(index) {
    const doc = currentResults[index];
    if (!doc) return;
    
    const detailTable = document.querySelector('#detail-table tbody');
    detailTable.innerHTML = '';
    
    const flatten = (obj, prefix = '') => {
        const rows = [];
        for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(obj)) {
            const full = prefix ? `${prefix}.${k}` : k;
            if (v && typeof v === 'object' && !Array.isArray(v)) {
                rows.push(...flatten(v, full));
            } else {
                rows.push({ key: full, value: v });
            }
        }
        return rows;
    };
    
    flatten(doc).forEach(r => {
        const tr = document.createElement('tr');
        tr.innerHTML = `<td>${r.key}</td><td>${typeof r.value==='object'?JSON.stringify
(r.value):r.value}</td>`;
        detailTable.appendChild(tr);
    });
    
    document.getElementById('detail-json').textContent = JSON.stringify(doc, null, 2);
    document.getElementById('detail-modal').classList.add('show');
    switchTab('table');
}
function closeDetailModal() { document.getElementById('detail-modal').classList.remove('s
how'); }
function switchTab(tab) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    event.target.classList.add('active');
    document.getElementById('detail-table-view').style.display = tab === 'table' ? 'bloc
k' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('detail-json-view').style.display = tab === 'json' ? 'block' 
: 'none';
}

function getTimeRangeStart(range) {
    const now = new Date();
    const map = { '15m': 15*60000, '1h': 3600000, '24h': 86400000, '7d': 7*86400000, '30
d': 30*86400000 };
    return map[range] ? new Date(now - map[range]).toISOString().slice(0,16) : '';
}

// ==================== EXPORT ====================
function exportCSV() {
    if (!currentResults.length) return alert('No data!');
    const headers = selectedColumns.map(c => c.name);
    const rows = currentResults.map(doc => 
        selectedColumns.map(c => {
            const v = getNestedValue(doc, c.name);
            return `"${String(v||'').replace(/"/g,'""')}"`;
        }).join(',')
    );
    downloadFile([headers.join(','), ...rows].join('\n'), 
        `wazuh-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.csv`, 'text/csv');
}
function exportJSON() {
    if (!currentResults.length) return alert('No data!');
    downloadFile(JSON.stringify(currentResults, null, 2), 
        `wazuh-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.json`, 'application/json');
}
function downloadFile(content, filename, type) {
    const blob = new Blob([content], { type });
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = filename;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);

// ==================== TOAST NOTIFICATION ====================
function showToast(message, type = 'info') {
    const existing = document.querySelector('.toast');
    if (existing) existing.remove();
    
    const toast = document.createElement('div');
    toast.className = `toast ${type}`;
    toast.textContent = message;
    document.body.appendChild(toast);
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        toast.style.animation = 'slideOut 0.3s ease forwards';
        setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 300);
    }, 2500);
}

    if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'Enter') executeSearch();
    if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 's') { e.preventDefault(); openSettings(); }
});

    },

        localStorage.removeItem('wazuh-soc-settings');
    }
};
// ==================== SEVERITY HELPERS ====================
function getSeverityLevel(level) {
    if (level >= 12) return 'critical';
    if (level >= 7) return 'high';
    if (level >= 4) return 'medium';
    if (level >= 1) return 'low';
    return 'info';
}
function getSeverityConfig(level) {
    const severity = getSeverityLevel(level);
    return CONFIG.SEVERITY[severity];
}
function getSeverityBadge(level) {
    const config = getSeverityConfig(level);
    return `<span class="severity-badge severity-${getSeverityLevel(level)}">
        <i class="fas fa-${config.icon} mr-1"></i> ${level}
    </span>`;
}
// ==================== UTILITY FUNCTIONS ====================
function formatTimestamp(ts) {
    if (!ts) return 'N/A';
    try {
        const date = new Date(ts);
        return date.toLocaleString('en-US', {
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'short',
            day: 'numeric',
            hour: '2-digit',
            minute: '2-digit',
            second: '2-digit',
            hour12: false
        });

    } catch { return ts; }
}
function formatBytes(bytes) {
    if (!bytes || bytes === 0) return '0 B';
    const k = 1024;
    const sizes = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
    const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
    return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + ' ' + sizes[i];
}
function formatNumber(num) {
    return num?.toLocaleString() || '0';
}
function getNestedValue(obj, path) {
    return path.split('.').reduce((current, key) => 
        (current && current[key] !== undefined) ? current[key] : null, obj);
}
function escapeHtml(text) {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = text || '';
    return div.innerHTML;
}
function truncate(text, maxLength = 100) {
    if (!text) return '';
    return text.length > maxLength ? text.substring(0, maxLength) + '...' : text;
}
function generateId() {
    return 'id_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
}
function debounce(func, wait) {
    let timeout;
    return function executedFunction(...args) {
        const later = () => {
            clearTimeout(timeout);
            func(...args);
        };
        clearTimeout(timeout);
        timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
    };
}
function throttle(func, limit) {
    let inThrottle;
    return function(...args) {
        if (!inThrottle) {
            func.apply(this, args);
            inThrottle = true;
            setTimeout(() => inThrottle = false, limit);
        }
    };
}

                           type === 'error' ? 'times-circle' : 
                           type === 'warning' ? 'exclamation-triangle' : 'info-circle'}">
</i>
            <span>${message}</span>
        </div>

// ==================== TIME RANGE HELPERS ====================
function getTimeRangeStart(range) {
    const now = new Date();
    switch(range) {
        case '15m': return new Date(now - 15 * 60000).toISOString();
        case '1h': return new Date(now - 3600000).toISOString();
        case '24h': return new Date(now - 86400000).toISOString();
        case '7d': return new Date(now - 7 * 86400000).toISOString();
        case '30d': return new Date(now - 30 * 86400000).toISOString();
        default: return null;
    }
}
// ==================== IOC DETECTION ====================
function detectIOCs(text) {
    if (!text || !STATE.iocTagging) return [];
    
    const iocs = [];
    const textStr = typeof text === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(text) : String(text);
    
    for (const [type, pattern] of Object.entries(CONFIG.IOC_PATTERNS)) {
        const matches = textStr.match(pattern);
        if (matches) {
            matches.forEach(match => {
                iocs.push({ type, value: match });
            });
        }
    }
    
    return iocs;
}

    async fetch(endpoint, params = {}, options = {}) {
        const url = new URL(`${CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}${endpoint}`);
        
        // Add query params
        Object.entries(params).forEach(([key, value]) => {
            if (value !== null && value !== undefined && value !== '') {
                url.searchParams.append(key, value);
            }
        });
        
        const controller = new AbortController();
        const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), options.timeout || 30000);
        
        try {
            const response = await fetch(url.toString(), {
                signal: controller.signal,
                ...options
            });
            
            clearTimeout(timeout);
            
            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}: ${response.statusText}`);
            }
            
            const data = await response.json();
            
            // Store for inspect
            STATE.lastRequestData = { url: url.toString(), params, options };
            STATE.lastResponseData = data;
            
            return data;
        } catch (error) {
            clearTimeout(timeout);
            if (error.name === 'AbortError') {
                throw new Error('Request timeout');
            }
            throw error;
        }
    },

    init() {
        const saved = Storage.load();
        if (!saved || !STATE.theme) {
            STATE.theme = CONFIG.DEFAULTS.theme;
        }
        this.applyTheme(STATE.theme);
        this.updateThemeUI();
    },
    
    applyTheme(theme) {
        STATE.theme = theme;
        
        const html = document.documentElement;
        const body = document.getElementById('body');
        
        switch(theme) {
            case 'dark':
                html.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
                html.classList.add('dark');
                html.classList.remove('light');
                break;
            case 'light':
                html.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
                html.classList.add('light');
                html.classList.remove('dark');
                break;
            case 'system':
                const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').mat
ches;
                html.setAttribute('data-theme', prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light');
                html.classList.toggle('dark', prefersDark);
                html.classList.toggle('light', !prefersDark);
                break;
        }
        
        this.updateThemeIcon();
        Storage.save();
    },
    
    toggleTheme() {
        const themes = ['dark', 'light', 'system'];
        const currentIndex = themes.indexOf(STATE.theme);
        const nextTheme = themes[(currentIndex + 1) % themes.length];
        this.applyTheme(nextTheme);
        this.updateThemeUI();
        showToast(`Theme: ${nextTheme.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + nextTheme.slice(1)}`, 'in
fo');
    },
    
    setTheme(theme) {
        this.applyTheme(theme);
        this.updateThemeUI();
        showToast(`Theme changed to ${theme}`, 'success');
    },
    
    updateThemeIcon() {
        const icon = document.getElementById('theme-icon');
        if (!icon) return;
        
        switch(STATE.theme) {
            case 'dark':
                icon.className = 'fas fa-moon';
                break;
            case 'light':
                icon.className = 'fas fa-sun';
                break;
            case 'system':
                icon.className = 'fas fa-desktop';
                break;
        }
    },

// ==================== DQL PARSER & SEARCH ENGINE ====================
const SearchEngine = {
    // Parse DQL query string into structured filters
    parseDQL(queryString) {
        if (!queryString || !queryString.trim()) return { filters: [], freeText: '' };
        
        const filters = [];
        let remaining = queryString.trim();
        
        // Match patterns like: field:"value" OR field:value AND field:[min TO max]
        const patterns = [
            // field:"exact phrase"
            { regex: /(\w+(?:\.\w+)*)\s*:\s*"([^"]+)"/g, type: 'exact' },
            // field:[min TO max]
            { regex: /(\w+(?:\.\w+)*)\s*:\s*\[(\S+)\s+TO\s+(\S+)\]/g, type: 'range' },
            // field:value
            { regex: /(\w+(?:\.\w+)*)\s*:\s*(\S+)/g, type: 'term' },
        ];
        
        patterns.forEach(({ regex, type }) => {
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 122/178

--- Page 123 ---
            let match;
            while ((match = regex.exec(remaining)) !== null) {
                if (type === 'range') {
                    filters.push({
                        field: match[1],
                        type: 'range',
                        min: match[2],
                        max: match[3],
                        operator: 'AND'
                    });
                } else {
                    filters.push({
                        field: match[1],
                        type: type,
                        value: match[2],
                        operator: 'AND'
                    });
                }
            }
        });
        
        // Extract operators (AND, OR, NOT)
        const operatorMatches = remaining.match(/\b(AND|OR|NOT)\b/g);
        if (operatorMatches) {
            operatorMatches.forEach((op, i) => {
                if (filters[i + 1]) {
                    filters[i + 1].operator = op;
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Get remaining free text
        let freeText = remaining;
        patterns.forEach(({ regex }) => {
            freeText = freeText.replace(regex, '');
        });
        freeText = freeText.replace(/\b(AND|OR|NOT)\b/g, '').trim();
        
        return { filters, freeText };
    },
    
    // Build Elasticsearch query from DQL
    buildESQuery(dqlString) {
        const { filters, freeText } = this.parseDQL(dqlString);
        const must = [];
        const should = [];
        const mustNot = [];
        
        filters.forEach(filter => {
            const condition = this.buildCondition(filter);
            
            switch(filter.operator) {
                case 'AND':
                    must.push(condition);
                    break;
                case 'OR':
                    should.push(condition);
                    break;
                case 'NOT':
                    mustNot.push(condition);
                    break;
                default:
                    must.push(condition);
            }
        });
        
        if (freeText) {
            must.push({
                query_string: {
                    query: freeText,
                    default_operator: 'AND'
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 123/178

--- Page 124 ---
                }
            });
        }
        
        const boolQuery = {};
        if (must.length) boolQuery.must = must;
        if (should.length) boolQuery.should = should;
        if (mustNot.length) boolQuery.must_not = mustNot;
        
        return Object.keys(boolQuery).length ? { bool: boolQuery } : { match_all: {} };
    },
    
    buildCondition(filter) {
        switch(filter.type) {
            case 'exact':
                return { match_phrase: { [filter.field]: filter.value } };
            case 'term':
                // Check if value is numeric
                if (!isNaN(filter.value)) {
                    return { term: { [filter.field]: Number(filter.value) } };
                }
                return { match: { [filter.field]: filter.value } };
            case 'range':
                const range = {};
                if (filter.min && filter.min !== '*') range.gte = isNaN(filter.min) ? fil
ter.min : Number(filter.min);
                if (filter.max && filter.max !== '*') range.lte = isNaN(filter.max) ? fil
ter.max : Number(filter.max);
                return { range: { [filter.field]: range } };
            default:
                return { match: { [filter.field]: filter.value } };
        }
    },
    
    // Execute search
    async execute() {
        const dqlInput = document.getElementById('dql-search-input');
        STATE.currentDQL = dqlInput?.value?.trim() || '';
        STATE.currentPage = 1;
        
        await executeSearch();
    },
    
    // Clear search
    clear() {
        document.getElementById('dql-search-input').value = '';
        STATE.currentDQL = '';
        STATE.activeFilters = [];
        STATE.currentPage = 1;
        updateActiveFiltersBar();
        executeSearch();
    },
    
    // Save current query

        }
        
        STATE.savedQueries.push({
            id: generateId(),

            query,

// ==================== SEARCH EXECUTION ====================
async function executeSearch(silent = false) {
    if (STATE.selectedIndices.length === 0) {
        if (!silent) showToast('Please select at least one index pattern', 'warning');
        return;
    }
    
    if (!silent) showLoading(true);
    STATE.searchStartTime = Date.now();
    
    try {
        const data = await API.search();
        
        if (data.success) {
            STATE.currentResults = data.results || [];
            STATE.totalHits = data.total || 0;
            STATE.totalPages = Math.ceil(STATE.totalHits / STATE.pageSize) || 1;
            STATE.lastSearchTime = Date.now() - STATE.searchStartTime;
            
            renderTable();
            updatePagination();
            updateResultsInfo();
            updateStatsBar();
            
            if (STATE.inspectMode) {
                updateInspectPanel();
            }
        } else {
            if (!silent) showToast('Search failed: ' + (data.error || 'Unknown error'), 
'error');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Search error:', error);
        if (!silent) showToast('Connection failed. Check API status.', 'error');
        updateConnectionStatus(false);
    } finally {
        if (!silent) showLoading(false);
    }
}

    executeSearch();

// ==================== AUTO REFRESH ====================
function setAutoRefresh(seconds) {
    STATE.autoRefreshSeconds = parseInt(seconds);
    
    if (STATE.autoRefreshTimer) clearInterval(STATE.autoRefreshTimer);
    if (STATE.countdownTimer) clearInterval(STATE.countdownTimer);
    
    if (STATE.autoRefreshSeconds > 0) {
        startAutoRefresh();
        showToast(`Auto-refresh: ${formatSeconds(STATE.autoRefreshSeconds)}`, 'success');
    } else {
        document.getElementById('refresh-status') && 
            (document.getElementById('refresh-status').textContent = 'Auto-refresh: OF
F');
    }
    
    Storage.save();
}
function startAutoRefresh() {
    let remaining = STATE.autoRefreshSeconds;
    
    STATE.countdownTimer = setInterval(() => {
        remaining--;
        updateCountdownDisplay(remaining);
        
        if (remaining <= 0) {
            remaining = STATE.autoRefreshSeconds;
        }
    }, 1000);
    
    STATE.autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(() => {
        if (STATE.selectedIndices.length > 0) {
            executeSearch(true);
        }
        remaining = STATE.autoRefreshSeconds;
    }, STATE.autoRefreshSeconds * 1000);
}
function updateCountdownDisplay(remaining) {
    const el = document.getElementById('refresh-status');
    if (el) {
        el.innerHTML = `Next refresh: <strong>${formatSeconds(remaining)}</strong>`;
    }
}
function formatSeconds(s) {
    if (s < 60) return `${s}s`;
    const m = Math.floor(s / 60);
    const sec = s % 60;
    return sec > 0 ? `${m}m ${sec}s` : `${m}m`;
}
