function updateResultsInfo() {
    const showingStart = document.getElementById('showing-start');
    const showingEnd = document.getElementById('showing-end');
    const totalHits = document.getElementById('total-hits');
    const pageIndicator = document.getElementById('page-indicator');
    
    if (showingStart) showingStart.textContent = STATE.currentResults.length > 0 ? 
        ((STATE.currentPage - 1) * STATE.pageSize + 1).toLocaleString() : '0';
    if (showingEnd) showingEnd.textContent = Math.min(
        STATE.currentPage * STATE.pageSize, STATE.totalHits
    ).toLocaleString();
    if (totalHits) totalHits.textContent = STATE.totalHits.toLocaleString();
    if (pageIndicator) pageIndicator.textContent = `Page ${STATE.currentPage} of ${STATE.
totalPages || 1}`;
    
    document.getElementById('last-refresh-sidebar') && 
        (document.getElementById('last-refresh-sidebar').textContent = 'Just now');

// ==================== FILTER MANAGER ====================
const FilterManager = {
    // Add a filter
    add(field, value, operator = 'is', label = null) {
        // Check if filter already exists
        const existingIndex = STATE.activeFilters.findIndex(
            f => f.field === field && f.value === value
        );
        
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
            showToast('Filter already exists', 'warning');
            return;
        }
        
        STATE.activeFilters.push({
            id: generateId(),
            field,
            value,
            operator,
            label: label || `${field}: ${value}`,
            negate: false,
        });
        
        this.updateUI();
        executeSearch();
        Storage.save();
    },
    
    // Remove a filter
    remove(filterId) {
        STATE.activeFilters = STATE.activeFilters.filter(f => f.id !== filterId);
        this.updateUI();
        executeSearch();
        Storage.save();
    },
    
    // Toggle filter negation (include/exclude)
    toggleNegate(filterId) {
        const filter = STATE.activeFilters.find(f => f.id === filterId);
        if (filter) {
            filter.negate = !filter.negate;
            this.updateUI();
            executeSearch();
            Storage.save();
        }
    },
    
    // Clear all filters
    clearAll() {
        STATE.activeFilters = [];
        this.updateUI();
        executeSearch();
        Storage.save();
    },
    
    // Pin filter to query (convert to DQL)
    pinToQuery(filterId) {
        const filter = STATE.activeFilters.find(f => f.id === filterId);
        if (filter) {
            const dqlInput = document.getElementById('dql-search-input');
            const currentValue = dqlInput.value.trim();
            const filterString = filter.negate ? 
                `NOT ${filter.field}:"${filter.value}"` : 
                `${filter.field}:"${filter.value}"`;
            
            dqlInput.value = currentValue ? 
                `${currentValue} AND ${filterString}` : 
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 129/178

--- Page 130 ---
                filterString;
            
            STATE.currentDQL = dqlInput.value;
            this.remove(filterId);
        }
    },
    
    // Update filter bar UI
    updateUI() {
        const container = document.getElementById('active-filters-bar');
        if (!container) return;
        
        if (STATE.activeFilters.length === 0) {
            container.innerHTML = '<span class="text-xs opacity-40 italic">No active filt
ers. Click on field values to filter.</span>';
            return;
        }
        
        container.innerHTML = STATE.activeFilters.map(filter => `
            <span class="filter-chip ${filter.negate ? 'line-through opacity-60' : ''}" 
                  title="Click to negate, right-click for options">
                <span class="font-semibold text-blue-400">${filter.field}:</span>
                <span>${filter.negate ? 'NOT ' : ''}${truncate(filter.value, 30)}</span>
                <span class="remove-filter" onclick="FilterManager.remove('${filter.i
d}')" title="Remove filter">×</span>
            </span>
        `).join('');
        
        // Add clear all button
        container.innerHTML += `
            <button onclick="FilterManager.clearAll()" 
                    class="text-xs text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 px-2 py-1 rounded tran
sition">
                Clear all
            </button>
        `;
    },
    
    // Build query from filters
    buildQueryFromFilters() {
        if (STATE.activeFilters.length === 0) return '';
        
        return STATE.activeFilters.map(f => {
            const prefix = f.negate ? 'NOT ' : '';
            return `${prefix}${f.field}:"${f.value}"`;
        }).join(' AND ');
    },
};
// ==================== QUICK FILTER FROM TABLE CLICK ====================
function addQuickFilter(field, value) {
    FilterManager.add(field, value);
}
function addExcludeFilter(field, value) {
    FilterManager.add(field, value, 'is_not');
    const filter = STATE.activeFilters[STATE.activeFilters.length - 1];
    if (filter) filter.negate = true;
    FilterManager.updateUI();
    executeSearch();
    Storage.save();
}

// ==================== TIME RANGE ====================
function setTimeRange(range) {
    STATE.timeRange = range;
    
    // Update button styles
    document.querySelectorAll('.time-btn').forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.remove('active', 'bg-blue-600', 'text-white');
    });
    
    // Find and activate the clicked button
    const activeBtn = document.querySelector(`.time-btn[onclick*="${range}"]`);
    if (activeBtn) {
        activeBtn.classList.add('active', 'bg-blue-600', 'text-white');
    }
    
    // Clear custom time inputs if preset selected
    if (range !== 'custom') {
        document.getElementById('custom-time-start').value = '';
        document.getElementById('custom-time-end').value = '';
        STATE.customStartTime = null;
        STATE.customEndTime = null;
    }
    
    if (STATE.selectedIndices.length > 0) {
        STATE.currentPage = 1;
        executeSearch();
    }
    
    Storage.save();
}

// ==================== FIELD EXPLORER ====================
const FieldExplorer = {
    // Load available fields for selected indices
    async loadFields() {
        if (STATE.selectedIndices.length === 0) return;
        
        try {
            const indexPattern = STATE.selectedIndices.join(',');
            const data = await API.getFields(indexPattern);
            
            if (data.success && data.fields) {
                STATE.availableFields = data.fields.map(f => ({
                    ...f,
                    selected: STATE.selectedColumns.some(c => c.name === f.name),
                    pinned: STATE.pinnedFields.includes(f.name),
                    favorite: STATE.favoriteFields.includes(f.name),
                }));
                
                this.render();
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Failed to load fields:', error);
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 132/178

--- Page 133 ---
        }
    },
    
    // Render field explorer in sidebar
    render() {
        const container = document.getElementById('field-explorer-list');
        if (!container) return;
        
        const searchTerm = document.getElementById('field-search-input')?.value?.toLowerC
ase() || '';
        
        let fields = STATE.availableFields;
        
        // Filter by search
        if (searchTerm) {
            fields = fields.filter(f => f.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm));
        }
        
        // Sort: pinned first, then favorites, then selected, then alphabetical
        fields.sort((a, b) => {
            if (a.pinned && !b.pinned) return -1;
            if (!a.pinned && b.pinned) return 1;
            if (a.favorite && !b.favorite) return -1;
            if (!a.favorite && b.favorite) return 1;
            if (a.selected && !b.selected) return -1;
            if (!a.selected && b.selected) return 1;
            return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
        });
        
        // Group fields by category
        const categories = {
            'Pinned': fields.filter(f => f.pinned),
            'Favorites': fields.filter(f => f.favorite && !f.pinned),
            'Selected': fields.filter(f => f.selected && !f.pinned && !f.favorite),
            'Available': fields.filter(f => !f.selected && !f.pinned && !f.favorite),
        };
        
        let html = '';
        
        for (const [category, categoryFields] of Object.entries(categories)) {
            if (categoryFields.length === 0) continue;
            
            html += `<div class="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider opaci
ty-40 px-2 py-1 mt-2">${category}</div>`;
            
            categoryFields.slice(0, 50).forEach(field => {
                const icon = field.pinned ? ' 📌 ' : field.favorite ? ' ⭐ ' : field.selecte
d ? ' ✅ ' : ' ➕ ';
                html += `
                    <div class="field-item ${field.selected ? 'selected' : ''}" 
                         onclick="FieldExplorer.toggleField('${field.name}')"
                         oncontextmenu="event.preventDefault(); FieldExplorer.showFieldCo
ntextMenu(event, '${field.name}')"
                         title="${field.name} (${field.type})">
                        <span class="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <span>${icon}</span>
                            <span class="font-mono">${field.name}</span>
                        </span>
                        <span class="field-count">${field.type || 'unknown'}</span>
                    </div>
                `;
            });
        }
        
        container.innerHTML = html || '<div class="text-xs opacity-50 text-center py-4">N
o fields found</div>';
    },
    
    // Toggle field selection (add/remove from table columns)
    toggleField(fieldName) {
        const existingIndex = STATE.selectedColumns.findIndex(c => c.name === fieldName);

// ==================== TABLE RENDERER ====================
const TableRenderer = {
    // Main table render
    render() {

        this.renderBody();

    // Format cell value based on field type
    formatCellValue(value, fieldName, fullDoc) {
        if (value === null || value === undefined) {
            return '<span class="text-gray-500 italic">-</span>';
        }
        
        // Rule level - severity badge
        if (fieldName === 'rule.level') {
            return getSeverityBadge(parseInt(value));
        }
        
        // Timestamp
        if (fieldName === 'timestamp' || fieldName === '@timestamp') {
            return `<span class="font-mono text-xs">${formatTimestamp(value)}</span>`;
        }

            }

            </span>`;

        // Index name
        if (fieldName === '_index') {
            return `<span class="text-xs opacity-60">${escapeHtml(String(value).split('-
').pop())}</span>`;
        }
        
        // Boolean values
        if (typeof value === 'boolean') {
            return `<span class="${value ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'}">
                <i class="fas fa-${value ? 'check' : 'times'}-circle"></i> ${value}
            </span>`;
        }
        
        // Objects
        if (typeof value === 'object') {
            return `<span class="text-xs font-mono opacity-60">{…}</span>`;
        }
        
        // Default
        return escapeHtml(truncate(String(value), 100));
    },

    // Infinite scroll handler
    setupInfiniteScroll() {
        const trigger = document.getElementById('infinite-scroll-trigger');
        if (!trigger) return;
        
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting && STATE.currentPage < STATE.totalPages) {
                    STATE.currentPage++;
                    executeSearch(true).then(() => {
                        // Append results instead of replacing
                        this.appendResults();
                    });
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.1 });
        
        observer.observe(trigger);
    },
    
    // Append results for infinite scroll
    appendResults() {
        const tbody = document.getElementById('log-table-body');
        if (!tbody || !STATE.currentResults) return;
        
        const startIndex = (STATE.currentPage - 1) * STATE.pageSize;
        
        const newRows = STATE.currentResults.map((doc, i) => {
            const globalIndex = startIndex + i + 1;
            const level = doc.rule?.level || 0;
            const severity = getSeverityLevel(level);
            const rowClass = STATE.severityHighlight ? `row-${severity}` : '';
            
            let rowHtml = `<tr class="${rowClass} group cursor-pointer" 
                               onclick="viewDocument(${i})"
                               id="row-${globalIndex}">`;
            
            STATE.selectedColumns.forEach(col => {
                const value = getNestedValue(doc, col.name);
                rowHtml += `<td>${this.formatCellValue(value, col.name, doc)}</td>`;
            });
            
            rowHtml += `<td class="text-center text-xs opacity-40">${globalIndex}</td>`;
            rowHtml += '</tr>';
            
            return rowHtml;
        }).join('');
        
        tbody.innerHTML += newRows;
    },
};

function updatePagination() {
    const pageIndicator = document.getElementById('page-indicator');
    if (pageIndicator) {
        pageIndicator.textContent = `Page ${STATE.currentPage} of ${STATE.totalPages || 
1}`;
    }
    
    // Update showing numbers
    const showingStart = document.getElementById('showing-start');
    const showingEnd = document.getElementById('showing-end');
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 140/178

--- Page 141 ---
    const totalHitsEl = document.getElementById('total-hits');
    
    if (showingStart) {
        showingStart.textContent = STATE.currentResults.length > 0 ? 
            ((STATE.currentPage - 1) * STATE.pageSize + 1).toLocaleString() : '0';
    }
    if (showingEnd) {
        showingEnd.textContent = Math.min(
            STATE.currentPage * STATE.pageSize, STATE.totalHits
        ).toLocaleString();
    }
    if (totalHitsEl) {
        totalHitsEl.textContent = STATE.totalHits.toLocaleString();
    }
    
    // Disable/enable pagination buttons
    const btnFirst = document.querySelector('.pagination-btn:first-child');
    const btnPrev = document.querySelectorAll('.pagination-btn')[1];
    const btnNext = document.querySelectorAll('.pagination-btn')[2];
    const btnLast = document.querySelector('.pagination-btn:last-child');
    
    [btnFirst, btnPrev].forEach(btn => {
        if (btn) btn.disabled = STATE.currentPage <= 1;
    });
    [btnNext, btnLast].forEach(btn => {
        if (btn) btn.disabled = STATE.currentPage >= STATE.totalPages;
    });
}
function goToPage(page) {
    if (page < 1 || page > STATE.totalPages || page === STATE.currentPage) return;
    STATE.currentPage = page;
    executeSearch();
    document.getElementById('log-table-container')?.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' 
});
}
function nextPage() {
    if (STATE.currentPage < STATE.totalPages) {
        STATE.currentPage++;
        executeSearch();
        document.getElementById('log-table-container')?.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smo
oth' });
    }
}
function previousPage() {
    if (STATE.currentPage > 1) {
        STATE.currentPage--;
        executeSearch();
        document.getElementById('log-table-container')?.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smo
oth' });
    }
}
// ==================== SORTING ====================
function sortTable(field) {
    if (STATE.sortField === field) {
        STATE.sortOrder = STATE.sortOrder === 'desc' ? 'asc' : 'desc';
    } else {
        STATE.sortField = field;
        STATE.sortOrder = 'desc';
    }
    executeSearch();
    Storage.save();
}

// ==================== TIMELINE CHART ====================
const Timeline = {
    init() {
        this.canvas = document.getElementById('timeline-chart');
        if (!this.canvas) return;
        
        this.ctx = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
        this.data = [];
        this.resizeCanvas();
        
        window.addEventListener('resize', () => this.resizeCanvas());
    },
    
    resizeCanvas() {
        if (!this.canvas) return;
        const rect = this.canvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
        this.canvas.width = rect.width - 24;
        this.canvas.height = 128;
        this.draw();
    },
    
    // Build timeline data from search results
    buildData() {
        const timeBuckets = {};
        
        STATE.currentResults.forEach(doc => {
            if (!doc.timestamp) return;
            
            const date = new Date(doc.timestamp);
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 143/178

--- Page 144 ---
            const bucket = `${date.getFullYear()}-${String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart
(2, '0')}-${String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')} ${String(date.getHours()).padStart
(2, '0')}:${String(date.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
            
            if (!timeBuckets[bucket]) {
                timeBuckets[bucket] = { total: 0, critical: 0, high: 0, medium: 0, low: 
0, timestamp: date };
            }
            
            timeBuckets[bucket].total++;
            
            const level = doc.rule?.level || 0;
            if (level >= 12) timeBuckets[bucket].critical++;
            else if (level >= 7) timeBuckets[bucket].high++;
            else if (level >= 4) timeBuckets[bucket].medium++;
            else timeBuckets[bucket].low++;
        });
        
        this.data = Object.values(timeBuckets).sort((a, b) => a.timestamp - b.timestamp);
    },
    
    draw() {
        if (!this.ctx || this.data.length === 0) {
            this.drawEmpty();
            return;
        }
        
        const { width, height } = this.canvas;
        const ctx = this.ctx;
        
        // Clear
        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
        
        // Background
        ctx.fillStyle = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--bg
-secondary') || '#1e293b';
        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
        
        // Margins
        const margin = { top: 10, right: 10, bottom: 25, left: 40 };
        const chartWidth = width - margin.left - margin.right;
        const chartHeight = height - margin.top - margin.bottom;
        
        // Find max value
        const maxTotal = Math.max(...this.data.map(d => d.total), 1);
        
        // Draw grid lines
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
        for (let i = 0; i <= 4; i++) {
            const y = margin.top + (chartHeight * i / 4);
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.moveTo(margin.left, y);
            ctx.lineTo(width - margin.right, y);
            ctx.stroke();
        }
        
        // Draw bars
        const barWidth = Math.max(chartWidth / this.data.length - 1, 2);
        
        this.data.forEach((bucket, i) => {
            const x = margin.left + (chartWidth * i / this.data.length);
            const barHeight = (bucket.total / maxTotal) * chartHeight;
            const y = margin.top + chartHeight - barHeight;
            
            // Color based on severity
            const criticalRatio = bucket.critical / bucket.total;
            if (criticalRatio > 0.5) {
                ctx.fillStyle = '#dc2626';
            } else if (criticalRatio > 0.2 || bucket.high / bucket.total > 0.3) {
                ctx.fillStyle = '#ea580c';

            } else {
                ctx.fillStyle = '#3b82f6';
            }
            
            ctx.fillRect(x, y, barWidth, barHeight);
        });
        
        // Draw axes
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(margin.left, margin.top);
        ctx.lineTo(margin.left, margin.top + chartHeight);
        ctx.lineTo(width - margin.right, margin.top + chartHeight);
        ctx.stroke();
        
        // Labels
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)';
        ctx.font = '9px Inter, sans-serif';
        
        // Time labels
        const labelStep = Math.max(Math.floor(this.data.length / 4), 1);
        for (let i = 0; i < this.data.length; i += labelStep) {
            const x = margin.left + (chartWidth * i / this.data.length);
            const label = this.data[i].timestamp.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digi
t', minute: '2-digit' });
            ctx.fillText(label, x - 15, margin.top + chartHeight + 15);
        }
    },
    
    drawEmpty() {
        if (!this.ctx) return;
        const { width, height } = this.canvas;
        const ctx = this.ctx;
        
        ctx.fillStyle = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--bg
-secondary') || '#1e293b';
        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
        
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.3)';
        ctx.font = '12px Inter, sans-serif';
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.fillText('No timeline data', width / 2, height / 2);
        ctx.textAlign = 'start';
    },
    
    update() {
        this.buildData();
        this.resizeCanvas();
    }
};

// ==================== GEOLOCATION MAP ====================
const GeoMap = {
    init() {
        const mapEl = document.getElementById('geo-map');
        if (!mapEl) return;
        
        // Initialize Leaflet map
        this.map = L.map('geo-map', {
            center: [20, 0],
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 145/178

--- Page 146 ---
            zoom: 2,
            zoomControl: false,
            attributionControl: false,
        });
        
        // Add tile layer
        L.tileLayer('https://{s}.basemaps.cartocdn.com/dark_all/{z}/{x}/{y}{r}.png', {
            maxZoom: 19,
        }).addTo(this.map);
        
        this.markers = [];
        this.heatLayer = null;
    },
    
    // Update map with geo data
    async update() {
        if (!this.map) return;
        
        try {
            const geoData = await API.getGeoData();
            
            // Clear existing markers
            this.markers.forEach(m => this.map.removeLayer(m));
            this.markers = [];
            
            if (geoData.length === 0) {
                this.map.setView([20, 0], 2);
                return;
            }
            
            // Group by location
            const locations = {};
            geoData.forEach(point => {
                const key = `${point.lat.toFixed(2)},${point.lon.toFixed(2)}`;
                if (!locations[key]) {
                    locations[key] = { ...point, count: 0, maxLevel: 0 };
                }
                locations[key].count++;
                locations[key].maxLevel = Math.max(locations[key].maxLevel, point.level);
            });
            
            // Add markers
            Object.values(locations).forEach(loc => {
                const size = Math.min(loc.count * 3 + 8, 30);
                const color = loc.maxLevel >= 12 ? '#dc2626' :
                             loc.maxLevel >= 7 ? '#ea580c' :
                             loc.maxLevel >= 4 ? '#f59e0b' : '#22c55e';
                
                const marker = L.circleMarker([loc.lat, loc.lon], {
                    radius: size,
                    fillColor: color,
                    color: '#fff',
                    weight: 1,
                    opacity: 1,
                    fillOpacity: 0.7,
                }).addTo(this.map);
                
                marker.bindPopup(`
                    <div style="font-size:12px;">
                        <strong>${loc.city || 'Unknown'}, ${loc.country || 'Unknown'}</st
rong><br>
                        Events: ${loc.count}<br>
                        Max Level: ${loc.maxLevel}<br>
                        IP: ${loc.ip || 'N/A'}
                    </div>
                `);
                
                this.markers.push(marker);
            });
            
            // Fit bounds

    // Collect report data
    collectReportData() {
        // Calculate stats from current results or all data
        const stats = {
            critical: 0,
            high: 0,
            medium: 0,
            low: 0,
            total: STATE.totalHits,
        };
        
        STATE.currentResults.forEach(doc => {
            const level = doc.rule?.level || 0;
            if (level >= 12) stats.critical++;
            else if (level >= 7) stats.high++;
            else if (level >= 4) stats.medium++;
            else if (level >= 1) stats.low++;
        });
        
        // Top rules
        const ruleCounts = {};
        STATE.currentResults.forEach(doc => {
            const ruleId = doc.rule?.id || 'Unknown';
            if (!ruleCounts[ruleId]) {
                ruleCounts[ruleId] = {
                    id: ruleId,
                    description: doc.rule?.description || 'N/A',
                    level: doc.rule?.level || 0,
                    count: 0
                };
            }
            ruleCounts[ruleId].count++;
        });
        
        const topRules = Object.values(ruleCounts)
            .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
            .slice(0, 10);
        
        // Top agents
        const agentCounts = {};
        STATE.currentResults.forEach(doc => {
            const agentName = doc.agent?.name || 'Unknown';
            if (!agentCounts[agentName]) {
                agentCounts[agentName] = {
                    name: agentName,
                    count: 0,
                    lastEvent: doc.timestamp || 'N/A'
                };
            }
            agentCounts[agentName].count++;
            if (doc.timestamp > agentCounts[agentName].lastEvent) {
                agentCounts[agentName].lastEvent = doc.timestamp;
            }
        });
        
        const topAgents = Object.values(agentCounts)
            .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
            .slice(0, 10);
        
        // Recent critical & high alerts
        const recentAlerts = STATE.currentResults
            .filter(doc => (doc.rule?.level || 0) >= 7)
            .slice(0, 20)
            .map(doc => ({
                timestamp: doc.timestamp,
                level: doc.rule?.level || 0,
                ruleId: doc.rule?.id || 'N/A',
                description: doc.rule?.description || 'N/A',
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek

                agent: doc.agent?.name || 'N/A',

        let period = 'All time';

            period = `${new Date(STATE.customStartTime).toLocaleDateString()} - ${new Dat
e(STATE.customEndTime).toLocaleDateString()}`;

            topRules,
            topAgents,

function viewDocument(index) {
    const doc = STATE.currentResults[index];
    if (!doc) return;
    
    // Store current document
    window._currentDetailDoc = doc;
    
    // Show modal
    const modal = document.getElementById('document-detail-modal');
    modal.classList.remove('hidden');
    modal.classList.add('flex');
    
    // Render table view
    renderDocTableView(doc);
    
    // Render JSON view
    document.getElementById('doc-json-content').textContent = JSON.stringify(doc, null, 
2);
    
    // Render tree view
    document.getElementById('doc-tree-content').innerHTML = buildTreeView(doc);
    
    // Switch to table tab by default
    switchDocTab('table');
    
    // Highlight JSON
    if (window.CodeMirror) {
        // Could integrate CodeMirror for syntax highlighting
    }
}
function closeDocumentModal() {
    document.getElementById('document-detail-modal').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('document-detail-modal').classList.remove('flex');
}
function switchDocTab(tab) {
    // Update tab buttons
    document.querySelectorAll('.doc-tab-btn').forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.remove('border-blue-600', 'text-blue-600');
        btn.classList.add('border-transparent');
    });
    
    const activeTab = document.querySelector(`.doc-tab-btn[onclick*="${tab}"]`);
    if (activeTab) {
        activeTab.classList.add('border-blue-600', 'text-blue-600');
        activeTab.classList.remove('border-transparent');
    }
    
    // Show/hide views
    document.getElementById('doc-table-view').classList.toggle('hidden', tab !== 'tabl
e');
    document.getElementById('doc-json-view').classList.toggle('hidden', tab !== 'json');
    document.getElementById('doc-tree-view').classList.toggle('hidden', tab !== 'tree');
}

5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek

--- Page 153 ---
    const flattenObject = (obj, prefix = '') => {
        const rows = [];
        for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
            const fullKey = prefix ? `${prefix}.${key}` : key;
            if (key.startsWith('_')) continue; // Skip internal fields
            
            if (value && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
                rows.push(...flattenObject(value, fullKey));
            } else {
                let displayValue = value;
                if (Array.isArray(value)) {
                    displayValue = value.join(', ');
                } else if (typeof value === 'object') {
                    displayValue = JSON.stringify(value);
                }
                rows.push({ key: fullKey, value: displayValue });
            }
        }
        return rows;
    };
    
    const flatData = flattenObject(doc);
    
    flatData.forEach(row => {
        const tr = document.createElement('tr');
        tr.innerHTML = `
            <td class="font-semibold text-blue-500 font-mono text-xs py-2 px-3 border-b">
${row.key}</td>
            <td class="py-2 px-3 border-b text-sm">${escapeHtml(String(row.value ?? 'nul
l'))}</td>
        `;
        tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
}
function buildTreeView(obj, depth = 0) {
    if (obj === null) return '<span class="tree-node-value-null">null</span>';
    if (typeof obj !== 'object') {
        let cls = 'tree-node-value';
        if (typeof obj === 'string') cls += ' tree-node-value-string';
        else if (typeof obj === 'number') cls += ' tree-node-value-number';
        else if (typeof obj === 'boolean') cls += ' tree-node-value-boolean';
        return `<span class="${cls}">${JSON.stringify(obj)}</span>`;
    }
    
    if (Array.isArray(obj)) {
        if (obj.length === 0) return '<span class="tree-node-value">[]</span>';
        return `<details open>
            <summary class="tree-node-toggle">Array [${obj.length}]</summary>
            <div class="tree-node-children">
                ${obj.map((item, i) => `
                    <div><span class="tree-node-key">${i}:</span> ${buildTreeView(item, d
epth + 1)}</div>
                `).join('')}
            </div>
        </details>`;
    }
    
    const entries = Object.entries(obj);
    if (entries.length === 0) return '<span class="tree-node-value">{}</span>';
    
    return `<details open>
        <summary class="tree-node-toggle">Object {${entries.length}}</summary>
        <div class="tree-node-children">
            ${entries.map(([key, value]) => `
                <div><span class="tree-node-key">${key}:</span> ${buildTreeView(value, de
pth + 1)}</div>
            `).join('')}
        </div>
    </details>`;
}

function copyDocumentJSON(index) {

Doc;

// ==================== WEBSOCKET MANAGER ====================
const WebSocketManager = {
    connect() {
        // WebSocket connection for live streaming
        // Note: Requires WebSocket server endpoint on Wazuh server
        
        const wsUrl = CONFIG.API_BASE_URL.replace('http', 'ws') + '/ws/live';
        
        try {
            this.ws = new WebSocket(wsUrl);
            
            this.ws.onopen = () => {
                console.log('WebSocket connected');
                STATE.wsReconnectAttempts = 0;
                showToast('Live stream connected', 'success', 2000);
                
                // Subscribe to indices
                this.subscribe(STATE.selectedIndices);
            };
            
            this.ws.onmessage = (event) => {
                try {
                    const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
                    this.handleMessage(data);
                } catch (e) {
                    console.error('WebSocket message parse error:', e);
                }
            };
            
            this.ws.onerror = (error) => {
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 154/178

--- Page 155 ---
                console.error('WebSocket error:', error);
            };
            
            this.ws.onclose = () => {
                console.log('WebSocket disconnected');
                
                // Auto reconnect
                if (STATE.liveMode && STATE.wsReconnectAttempts < 10) {
                    STATE.wsReconnectAttempts++;
                    const delay = Math.min(1000 * STATE.wsReconnectAttempts, 30000);
                    console.log(`Reconnecting in ${delay}ms (attempt ${STATE.wsReconnectA
ttempts})`);
                    
                    setTimeout(() => this.connect(), delay);
                }
            };
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('WebSocket connection failed:', error);
            
            // Fallback to polling
            if (STATE.liveMode) {
                this.startPolling();
            }
        }
    },
    
    disconnect() {
        if (this.ws) {
            this.ws.close();
            this.ws = null;
        }
        this.stopPolling();
    },
    
    subscribe(indices) {
        if (this.ws && this.ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
            this.ws.send(JSON.stringify({
                action: 'subscribe',
                indices: indices,
            }));
        }
    },
    
    handleMessage(data) {
        if (data.type === 'alert') {
            // New alert received
            this.processNewAlert(data.payload);
        } else if (data.type === 'stats') {
            // Stats update
            updateStatsBar();
        }
    },
    
    processNewAlert(alert) {
        // Add new alert to the top of results
        STATE.currentResults.unshift(alert);
        STATE.totalHits++;
        
        // Keep only current page size
        if (STATE.currentResults.length > STATE.pageSize * 2) {
            STATE.currentResults = STATE.currentResults.slice(0, STATE.pageSize);
        }
        
        // Update table if on first page
        if (STATE.currentPage === 1) {
            renderTable();
        }
        
        // Update stats
        updateStatsBar();

    // Polling fallback
    pollingTimer: null,
    
    startPolling() {
        this.stopPolling();

            if (STATE.selectedIndices.length > 0) {
                executeSearch(true);
            }
        }, STATE.autoRefreshSeconds > 0 ? STATE.autoRefreshSeconds * 1000 : 10000);
    },
    
    stopPolling() {
        if (this.pollingTimer) {
            clearInterval(this.pollingTimer);
            this.pollingTimer = null;
        }
    },
};

    def es_query(self, method, path, body=None):
        """Execute Elasticsearch query via curl"""

            '-X', method,
            '-H', f'Authorization: Basic {auth_str}',
            '-H', 'Content-Type: application/json',
            f'{INDEXER_URL}{path}'
        ]
        if body:
            cmd.extend(['-d', json.dumps(body)])
        
        try:

    # ==================== GET ALL INDICES ====================
    def get_indices(self):
        data = self.es_query('GET', '/_cat/indices?format=json&bytes=b&h=index,health,sta
tus,docs.count,store.size,pri.store.size')
        
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": data['error']}
        
        indices = []
        for idx in data:
            name = idx.get('index', '')
            if name.startswith('.'):
                continue
            
            indices.append({
                "name": name,
                "health": idx.get('health', 'unknown'),
                "status": idx.get('status', 'unknown'),
                "docs_count": int(idx.get('docs.count', 0)),
                "store_size": idx.get('store.size', '0'),
                "pri_store_size": idx.get('pri.store.size', '0'),
                "pattern": self._extract_pattern(name)
            })

        patterns = {}
        for idx in indices:
            pattern = idx['pattern']
            if pattern not in patterns:
                patterns[pattern] = {
                    "pattern": pattern,
                    "indices": [],
                    "total_docs": 0,
                    "count": 0
                }
            patterns[pattern]['indices'].append(idx)
            patterns[pattern]['total_docs'] += idx['docs_count']
            patterns[pattern]['count'] += 1
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "total_indices": len(indices),
            "patterns": list(patterns.values()),
            "all_indices": sorted([idx['name'] for idx in indices], reverse=True)
        }

    def _extract_pattern(self, name):
        parts = name.split('-')
        if len(parts) >= 3:
            if len(parts[2]) >= 8 and parts[2][:4].isdigit():  # Date pattern like 2026.0
5.14
                return '-'.join(parts[:2]) + '-*'
        if len(parts) >= 2:
            return parts[0] + '-*'
        return name + '*'
    
    # ==================== GET INDEX STATS ====================
    def get_index_stats(self, params):
        index_name = params.get('index', [''])[0]
        if not index_name:
            return {"success": False, "error": "Missing 'index' parameter"}
        
        data = self.es_query('GET', f'/{index_name}/_stats/docs,store')
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": data['error']}
        
        total = data.get('_all', {}).get('total', {})
        return {
            "success": True,
            "index": index_name,
            "docs_count": total.get('docs', {}).get('count', 0),
            "size_bytes": total.get('store', {}).get('size_in_bytes', 0)
        }
    
    # ==================== GET FIELD MAPPINGS ====================
    def get_fields(self, params):
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        
        data = self.es_query('GET', f'/{index_pattern}/_mapping')
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": data['error']}
        
        fields = []
        try:
            # Navigate through mapping structure
            for idx_name, idx_data in data.items():
                mappings = idx_data.get('mappings', {})
                properties = mappings.get('properties', {})
                
                def extract_fields(prefix, props, depth=0):
                    if depth > 10:  # Prevent infinite recursion
                        return
                    for field, info in props.items():
                        full_path = f"{prefix}.{field}" if prefix else field
                        if 'properties' in info:
                            extract_fields(full_path, info['properties'], depth + 1)
                        else:
                            fields.append({
                                "name": full_path,
                                "type": info.get('type', 'object')
                            })
                
                extract_fields('', properties)
                break  # Only first index mapping
        except Exception as e:
            pass
        
        # Remove duplicates and sort
        seen = set()
        unique_fields = []
        for f in fields:
            if f['name'] not in seen:
                seen.add(f['name'])
                unique_fields.append(f)
        
        return {

    # ==================== ADVANCED SEARCH WITH DQL SUPPORT ====================
    def search_documents(self, params):
        """Main search endpoint with DQL query support"""
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        query_text = params.get('q', [''])[0]
        limit = min(int(params.get('limit', ['50'])[0]), 500)
        offset = int(params.get('offset', ['0'])[0])
        sort_field = params.get('sort', ['timestamp'])[0]
        sort_order = params.get('order', ['desc'])[0]
        
        # Build ES query
        must = []
        
        # DQL Query parsing
        if query_text:
            must.extend(self._parse_dql_to_es(query_text))
        
        # Advanced filters from URL params
        for key, values in params.items():
            if key.startswith('filter_'):
                field = key.replace('filter_', '')
                value = values[0] if values else ''
                if value:
                    if field == 'rule.level':
                        must.append({"match": {"rule.level": value}})
                    elif field == 'rule.id':
                        must.append({"match": {"rule.id": value}})
                    elif field == 'agent.name':
                        must.append({"match": {"agent.name": value}})
                    else:
                        must.append({"match": {field: value}})
        
        # Rule level range filters
        rule_min = params.get('rule_level_min', [None])[0]
        rule_max = params.get('rule_level_max', [None])[0]
        if rule_min or rule_max:
            level_range = {}
            if rule_min:
                level_range['gte'] = int(rule_min)
            if rule_max:
                level_range['lte'] = int(rule_max)
            if level_range:
                must.append({"range": {"rule.level": level_range}})
        
        # Rule ID direct filter
        rule_id = params.get('rule_id', [None])[0]
        if rule_id:
            must.append({"match": {"rule.id": rule_id}})
        
        # Agent name filter
        agent_name = params.get('agent_name', [None])[0]
        if agent_name and agent_name != '*':
            must.append({"match": {"agent.name": agent_name}})
        
        # Date filters
        start_date = params.get('start_date', [None])[0]
        end_date = params.get('end_date', [None])[0]
        if start_date:
            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"gte": self._parse_date(start_date)}}})
        if end_date:
            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"lte": self._parse_date(end_date)}}})
        
        # Build final query
        query_dict = {
            "from": offset,
            "size": limit,
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94

--- Page 167 ---
            "sort": [{sort_field: {"order": sort_order}}],
            "query": {"bool": {"must": must}} if must else {"match_all": {}}
        }
        
        data = self.es_query('POST', f'/{index_pattern}/_search', query_dict)
        
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": str(data['error']), "query": query_dict}
        
        total = data.get('hits', {}).get('total', {})
        total_value = total.get('value', 0) if isinstance(total, dict) else total
        
        hits = data.get('hits', {}).get('hits', [])
        documents = []
        for hit in hits:
            doc = hit.get('_source', {})
            doc['_id'] = hit.get('_id', '')
            doc['_index'] = hit.get('_index', '')
            doc['_score'] = hit.get('_score', 0)
            documents.append(doc)
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "total": total_value,
            "offset": offset,
            "limit": limit,
            "count": len(documents),
            "results": documents
        }
    
    def _parse_dql_to_es(self, query_text):
        """Parse DQL-style query to Elasticsearch must clauses"""
        must = []
        
        if not query_text or query_text == '*':
            return must
        
        # Handle field:value patterns
        # Pattern: field.name:"exact phrase"
        phrase_pattern = re.findall(r'(\w+(?:\.\w+)*)\s*:\s*"([^"]+)"', query_text)
        for field, value in phrase_pattern:
            must.append({"match_phrase": {field: value}})
            query_text = query_text.replace(f'{field}:"{value}"', '')
        
        # Pattern: field.name:value
        term_pattern = re.findall(r'(\w+(?:\.\w+)*)\s*:\s*(\S+)', query_text)
        for field, value in term_pattern:
            # Skip if already matched as phrase
            if f'"{value}"' not in query_text:
                # Check if numeric
                try:
                    num_val = float(value)
                    must.append({"term": {field: num_val}})
                except ValueError:
                    must.append({"match": {field: value}})
                query_text = query_text.replace(f'{field}:{value}', '')
        
        # Handle range: field:[min TO max]
        range_pattern = re.findall(r'(\w+(?:\.\w+)*)\s*:\s*\[(\S+)\s+TO\s+(\S+)\]', query
_text)
        for field, min_val, max_val in range_pattern:
            range_query = {}
            if min_val != '*':
                try:
                    range_query['gte'] = float(min_val)
                except ValueError:
                    range_query['gte'] = min_val
            if max_val != '*':
                try:
                    range_query['lte'] = float(max_val)
                except ValueError:
5/24/26, 3:05 PM 100% working new dashborad unishield Wazuh API Dashboard Flow - DeepSeek
https://chat.deepseek.com/a/chat/s/0962c3b3-94b1-4242-95f3-645c98053447 167/178

--- Page 168 ---
                    range_query['lte'] = max_val
            if range_query:
                must.append({"range": {field: range_query}})
        
        # Handle remaining free text with query_string
        remaining = query_text.strip()
        # Remove boolean operators
        remaining = re.sub(r'\b(AND|OR|NOT)\b', '', remaining, flags=re.IGNORECASE).strip
()
        
        if remaining:
            must.append({
                "query_string": {
                    "query": remaining,
                    "default_operator": "AND"
                }
            })
        
        return must
    
    # ==================== COUNT DOCUMENTS ====================
    def count_documents(self, params):
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        query_text = params.get('q', [''])[0]
        
        # Build query similar to search
        must = self._parse_dql_to_es(query_text) if query_text else []
        
        query_dict = {"query": {"bool": {"must": must}}} if must else {"query": {"match_a
ll": {}}}
        
        data = self.es_query('POST', f'/{index_pattern}/_count', query_dict)
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "index": index_pattern,
            "query": query_text,
            "count": data.get('count', 0) if 'error' not in data else 0
        }
    
    # ==================== SCAN ALERTS (ORIGINAL ENDPOINT - KEPT FOR BACKWARD COMPATIBILI
TY) ====================
    def scan_alerts(self, params):
        min_level = int(params.get('min_level', ['1'])[0])
        max_level = int(params.get('max_level', ['15'])[0])
        start_date = params.get('start_date', [None])[0]
        end_date = params.get('end_date', [None])[0]
        event_id = params.get('event_id', [None])[0]
        rule_id = params.get('rule_id', [None])[0]
        description = params.get('description', [None])[0]
        limit = min(int(params.get('limit', ['500'])[0]), 2000)
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        
        must = [{"range": {"rule.level": {"gte": min_level, "lte": max_level}}}]
        
        if start_date:
            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"gte": self._parse_date(start_date)}}})
        if end_date:
            must.append({"range": {"timestamp": {"lte": self._parse_date(end_date)}}})
        if event_id:
            must.append({"term": {"data.win.system.eventID": event_id}})
        if rule_id:
            must.append({"match": {"rule.id": rule_id}})
        if description:
            must.append({"match": {"rule.description": description}})
        
        query_dict = {
            "size": limit,
            "sort": [{"timestamp": {"order": "desc"}}],
            "query": {"bool": {"must": must}}
        }

        data = self.es_query('POST', f'/{index_pattern}/_search', query_dict)

            alert = hit['_source']
            alert['_id'] = hit.get('_id', '')
            alert['_index'] = hit.get('_index', '')
            raw_alerts.append(alert)
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "total": total_value,
            "count": len(raw_alerts),
            "results": raw_alerts
        }
    
    # ==================== AGGREGATION ====================
    def aggregate_data(self, params):
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        agg_field = params.get('field', ['rule.level'])[0]
        agg_type = params.get('type', ['terms'])[0]  # terms, date_histogram
        limit = int(params.get('limit', ['20'])[0])
        
        if agg_type == 'terms':
            agg_query = {
                "size": 0,
                "aggs": {
                    "group_by": {
                        "terms": {
                            "field": agg_field,
                            "size": limit,
                            "order": {"_count": "desc"}
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        elif agg_type == 'date_histogram':
            interval = params.get('interval', ['1h'])[0]
            agg_query = {
                "size": 0,
                "aggs": {
                    "group_by": {
                        "date_histogram": {
                            "field": agg_field,
                            "calendar_interval": interval,
                            "order": {"_key": "desc"}
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        else:
            return {"success": False, "error": f"Unknown aggregation type: {agg_type}"}
        
        data = self.es_query('POST', f'/{index_pattern}/_search', agg_query)
        
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": str(data['error'])}
        
        buckets = data.get('aggregations', {}).get('group_by', {}).get('buckets', [])
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "field": agg_field,

            "type": agg_type,
            "buckets": buckets
        }
    
    # ==================== GEO DATA ====================
    def get_geo_data(self, params):
        index_pattern = params.get('index', ['wazuh-alerts-4.x-*'])[0]
        limit = min(int(params.get('limit', ['1000'])[0]), 5000)
        
        query_dict = {
            "size": limit,
            "query": {
                "bool": {
                    "must": [
                        {"exists": {"field": "data.geoip.location"}}
                    ]
                }
            },
            "_source": ["data.geoip", "data.srcip", "rule.level", "timestamp", "agent.nam
e"]
        }
        
        data = self.es_query('POST', f'/{index_pattern}/_search', query_dict)
        
        if 'error' in data:
            return {"success": False, "error": str(data['error'])}
        
        hits = data.get('hits', {}).get('hits', [])
        geo_docs = []
        for hit in hits:
            doc = hit.get('_source', {})
            geo = doc.get('data', {}).get('geoip', {})
            location = geo.get('location', {})
            
            if location:
                geo_docs.append({
                    "lat": location.get('lat'),
                    "lon": location.get('lon'),
                    "city": geo.get('city_name', 'Unknown'),
                    "country": geo.get('country_name', 'Unknown'),
                    "ip": doc.get('data', {}).get('srcip', 'N/A'),
                    "level": doc.get('rule', {}).get('level', 0),
                    "agent": doc.get('agent', {}).get('name', 'N/A'),
                    "timestamp": doc.get('timestamp', '')
                })
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "count": len(geo_docs),
            "results": geo_docs
        }
    
    # ==================== UTILITY ====================
    def _parse_date(self, date_str):
        if not date_str:
            return None
        # Handle already ISO format
        if 'T' in date_str:
            return date_str
        
        formats = [
            '%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M',
            '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M',
            '%Y-%m-%d',
            '%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S',
            '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S',
        ]
        for fmt in formats:
            try:
                return datetime.strptime(date_str, fmt).strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S')
            except:
